<form><strong style="color:darkred; font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size:14pt">瑜伽師地論科句披尋記卷第十</strong></form>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　彌勒菩薩說</span></span></span><br />
<a name="10p725"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　唐三藏沙門玄奘奉詔譯</span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　韓清淨科記</span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">本地分中有尋有伺等三地之七</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉的第七個部分，繼續卷9所說三雜染中的生雜染。前面說到緣起差別十二支中的受差別，現在從愛差別開始。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌八、愛差別3　亥一、欲愛</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科愛差別，愛的體性差別，分三科；第一科欲愛，說明欲界愛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="6814:7106"></a>欲愛云何？謂欲界諸行為緣所生，於欲界行染汙希求，由此能生欲界苦果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲愛是什麼？是指觸對欲界的五蘊等諸行生受為緣所生，對於欲界的五蘊、有情世間、及器世間諸行產生染污希求，由此造業而生出欲界的苦果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、色愛</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科色愛，說明色界的愛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">色愛云何？謂色界諸行為緣所生，於色界行染汙希求，由此能生色界苦果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　色愛是什麼？是指觸對色界的五蘊等諸行生受為緣所生，對於色界的三昧樂產生染污希求，由此造業而生出色界的苦果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、無色愛</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科無色愛，說明無色界的愛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">無色愛云何？謂無色界諸行為緣所生，於無色界行染汙希求，由此能生無色界苦果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無色愛是什麼？是指觸對無色界的受等四蘊等諸行生受為緣所生，於無色界定產生染污希求，由此造業而生出無色界的苦果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p726"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》欲愛色愛無色愛者：此中三愛，各有三相。一者、因相，二者、自相，三者、果相。言因相者，謂愛由緣境界受生，故說三界諸行為緣。言自相者，希求相是愛相，謂能發起諸取業故；或有是愛而非染汙，謂希求勝解脫，及依善愛而捨餘愛。為簡彼故，說於三界諸行染汙希求。言果相者，若彼彼處諸愛未斷，即彼彼處功能現前，能生後有，故說能生三界苦果。三愛差別，如文可知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這當中三種愛各有三相，包括因相、自相、及果相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　說因相，是指愛煩惱由緣境界受而生，緣受有愛，因此說三界諸行為緣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　說自相，是指希求相就是愛著相，有貪愛以後，就會產生種種的行動想要取得它，能發動諸取業故；或是有一種愛不是染汙心相應，不與無明相應的出離愛，希求殊勝的解脫，希求殊勝的善愛通常是指出家，想要出家修行，對於三界的愛就不再愛著，依善愛而棄捨其餘的愛。為了簡別希求勝解脫及善愛，而說對於三界諸行染污希求的愛。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　說果相，是指若是對於三界諸處的愛煩惱沒有斷除，愛種子還在阿賴耶識中，因緣具足時，在三界諸處功能現前，能生出後有的果報體。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果愛著欲界的境界，會得到欲界的苦果；愛著色界的境界，會得到色界的苦果；愛著無色界的境界，會得到無色界的苦果。三種愛的差別，如文所說可知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌九、取差別2　亥一、辨相4　天一、欲取</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科取差別，取的差別，分二科；第一科辨相，說明種種取的相貌，又分四科；第一科欲取，說明欲取的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">欲取云何？謂於諸欲所有欲貪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲取是什麼？是指為得到諸欲，及為了受用諸欲，對於所有欲的境界如色聲香味觸、男女等欲有貪，稱為欲貪。《俱舍論》卷10說：「世諸妙境非真欲，真欲謂人分別貪，妙境如本住世間，智者於中已除欲。」世間種種微妙的境界，不是真實的欲，因為這是外在的，所謂的欲，主要是內心的貪愛分別，有智慧的人已斷除欲貪，面對諸欲不會再生起欲貪分別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、見取</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科見取，說明見取的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">見取云何？謂除薩迦耶見，於所餘見所有欲貪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　見取是什麼？是指除了薩迦耶見，所餘的邊執見、邪見、戒禁取見等所有欲貪。依〈攝事分〉卷89，2650頁所說，由貪著利養及恭敬的增上力，或為詰問責難他所安立的論點，或是為免脫於他人的難問，而生起見取。為何稱為取？因為這類人取著邊執見、邪見等見解是最殊勝，最高尚的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、戒禁取</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科戒禁取，說明戒禁取的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戒禁取云何？謂於邪願所起戒禁所有欲貪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　戒禁取是什麼？是指由於有邪見相應的生天之願，所生起的身護、語護等戒禁所有欲貪，以為由此戒禁可以滿足生天之願，如印度的外道持牛戒、持狗戒等為生天之因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天四、我語取</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科我語取，說明我語取的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">我語取云何？謂於薩迦耶見所有欲貪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　我語取是什麼？是指對於自身，隨假言說，起於我執，隨執取著，所有的欲貪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p727"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》欲取見取戒禁取我語取者：當知此中，若所取、若能取、若所為取，如是一切總說為取。問：何所取？答：欲、見、戒禁、我語是所取。問：何能取？答：四種欲貪是能取。問：何所為取？答：為得諸欲及為受用，故起初取。由貪利養及以恭敬增上力故，或為詰責他所立論，或為免脫他所徵難，起第二取。奢摩他支為所依止為所建立，為欲往趣世間離欲乃至非想非非想處三摩鉢底，起第三取。為欲隨說分別所計作業受果所有士夫，及為隨說流轉還滅士夫之相，起我語取。如下攝事分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/89.htm#7122:68366">陵本八十九卷十頁6750</a>）今於此中略說所取、能取，如文可知。無所為取，然義定有，故應準釋。分別俱貪，名為欲貪，唯煩惱欲名為欲故。由是欲貪通三界有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道在這中間，若所取的境界，能取的欲貪，若所為取就是取的目的，這一切總說為取。問：什麼是欲貪所取的對象？答：欲，色聲香味觸男女等欲；見，種種錯誤的思想，如我見等；戒禁，所受持禁制身語的戒條；我語取，對於自身隨假言說，起於我執生起我見我慢等，這四種是所取。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：什麼是能取？答：於四種所取的境界產生的欲貪是能取。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：什麼是所為取？答：為了得到種種色聲香味觸男女諸欲，及為了受用這些境界，生起欲取；由於貪著利養及恭敬等增上力的原因，或是為了詰責難問他人所安立的言論，或是為了免於他人所難問，生起第二種的見取；依止奢摩他支所建立的禪定，為了要往趣世間離欲的色界定乃至無色界的非想非非想處的三摩鉢底，生起第三種戒禁取；為了要隨順世間人所說而分別計度執著造業受果所有的人，及為隨順所說流轉還滅聖者的相貌，生起第四種我語取。如〈攝事分〉卷89，2650頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　現在於此處要略說明所取、能取，如文中所說可以知道。雖然其中沒有明白的說所取的內容，然而其中一定是有的，所以應該準照那裏的解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能分別的心與貪煩惱同時活動，名為欲貪，但唯是有煩惱欲才名為欲，不是指事欲，因此說欲貪通三界有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、料簡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科料簡，重新思量簡擇說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">初唯能生欲界苦果，餘三通生三界苦果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種欲取對欲界諸行有染污希求，由此造業，能生欲界的苦果，其他戒禁取、見取、我語取三種通於三界，有這三種錯誤的取著，能生欲界、色界、無色界的苦果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》初唯能生欲界苦果等者：初一欲取唯欲界有，故說唯生欲界苦果。所餘三取通三界有，故說通生三界苦果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種欲取只有欲界才有，因此說唯生欲界苦果。其他見取、戒禁取、我語取三種取，通於三界，所以說通生三界苦果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p728"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌十、有差別2　亥一、別辨相3　天一、欲有2　地一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科有差別，有的體性差別，分二科；第一科別辨相，各別辨明三有的相貌，又分三科；第一科欲有，說明欲有的體相，又分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">欲有云何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲有是什麼？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、釋2　玄一、辨類</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科辨類，辨明欲有的類別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="52928:7130"></a>謂欲界本有、業有、死有、中有、生有，及那落迦、傍生、餓鬼、人、天有，總說名欲有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界的有，有本有、業有、死有、中有、生有，及那落迦、傍生、餓鬼、人、天有共十種，總說名為欲有。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有，是指存在、生存之義。欲界的欲有四種：一者情欲，二者色欲，三者食欲，四者婬欲。下極阿鼻地獄，上至第六他化天，男女相參，多諸染欲，稱為欲界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界本有，指欲界有情在生有與死有之間，業力壽命存續期間稱為本有。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　業有，又名為行有，指身口意所作善惡之業因，能招未來善惡之業果，因果不亡，故名業有。由染污希求諸欲造業而招感欲界的果報，名欲界的業有。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　死有，指本有之後，中有之前，五蘊業果色身一時壞滅，稱為死有。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　中有，也名中陰，指諸眾生此身死後，識未託胎，現在所作善惡業因，必取當來善惡諸趣之果，因果不亡，因此名中有。將來欲界受生的中有，名欲界中有；死有的同時就有一個中有生起，中有不是正式的果報，它是在死有與生有二有中間產生的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　生有，是指隨業識依中有入胎獲得下一世異熟果報體的一剎那。那落迦、傍生、餓鬼、人、天有，是指五趣的有。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《俱舍論》卷10說，佛陀以五種相說明中有：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、意成，指中有，由意所成，從意所生，也稱為意成身，不是父精母血等所有外緣所合成的；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、求生，中有常喜尋伺將要受生的處所；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、食香，也稱為尋香行。因為中有沒有段食，只能受用香味，以香為食；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、中有，是指二趣中間的五蘊生命體，中間的有稱為中有，只有清淨天眼才看得到。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、起，中有也稱為起，因為對向當生暫時起故，起是暫時生起的身體。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《契經》上說：「有壞自體起，有壞世間生」有壞是指有情的身體一定要先壞掉，中有才會生起，這個世間一定要壞滅世間才會不斷的產生。又說，「有補特伽羅，已斷起結，未斷生結。」這是說有些有情已經斷除欲界及色界中有的煩惱，可是還有無色界生有的煩惱沒有斷除，沒有中有的煩惱稱為已斷起結，還要到無色界去受生，稱為未斷生結。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、出體</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科出體，說名有的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復由先所作諸行煩惱攝受之所熏發。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這些「有」是由過去生所造作的種種業行，由愛取煩惱攝受之所熏發而成的異熟果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》欲有云何等者：除生剎那，死前餘位所有諸蘊，是名本有。業能引有，名為業有。死剎那位所有諸蘊，名為死有。死有、生有中間生故，名為中有。初生剎那，名為生有。業所引果有五趣別，由是建立那落迦有乃至天有。如是一切，若欲界繫，總名欲有。又復那落迦等五有，由先所作福非福行，及與愛、取煩惱攝受差別熏發方能現前，業果異熟理應爾故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　除了生的一剎那，一直到死以前所有的諸蘊，稱為本有。業力能引發有，稱為業有。死的一剎那位所有的諸蘊，稱為死有。死有與生有中間所生的，稱為中有。剛投生的一剎那，名為生有。業所引生的果報有五趣的差別，由此建立地獄有、餓鬼有、傍生有、人有、乃至天有。如是這一切有，都是屬於欲界所繫，總名為欲有。又地獄等五趣的有，是由過去所作的福行、非福行，及與愛煩惱、取煩惱所攝受的差別熏發才能現前，這是業果異熟的理則法爾如是。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、色有</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科色有，說明色界天的色有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p729"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">色有云何？謂除那落迦、傍生、餓鬼、人有，所餘是色有應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　色有是什麼？是指除了地獄、傍生、餓鬼、人有，所餘的是色（界天）有，包括本有、業有、死有、中有、生有、及天有。此處還應該簡除欲界天有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》色有云何等者：若色界繫本有、業有、死有、中有、生有、天有，總名色有應知。以色界非那落迦等生所依處，是故除之。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若繫屬於色界本有、業有、死有、中有、生有、天有，總名色有應當了知。因為色界不是地獄等生命所依處，因此簡除四種有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、無色有</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三無色有，說明無色界的無色有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">無色有云何？謂復除中有，所餘是無色有應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無色有是什麼？是指除了中有以外，所餘的本有、業有、死有、生有、天有五種是無色有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》無色有云何等者：無色界繫本有、業有、死有、生有、天有，名無色有。以無色界無中有生，故復除之。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　屬於無色界所繫的本有、業有、死有、生有、天有，名為無色有。由於無色界沒有中有生，因此除去中有。要到無色界去受生的人是沒有中有的，因為無色界沒有色身，所以那個人如果在哪裡修定，死的當處就是無色界受生處，稱為無色有。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無色界的生命型態到底是怎樣很難說，在部派佛教裡有爭議，有的部派覺得名色相依，生命體不可能沒有色，無色界的人還是有色，只是跟欲界有情的色不一樣，非常輕盈，不是麤色，一般人看不到的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　主張無色界天人還是有微細色的人說：經中說舍利佛死時，無色界天淚如細雨；像毛毛雨一樣，這就證明無色界天的人應該也有色。本論說， 無色界有情可以有定果色，沒有業果色。這種人要是來人間修行時想要聽佛說法，必需先變出一個色身才能坐下來聽法，若所變色身太輕會坐不住而飄起來，所以佛會要他們變出比較粗重的身體，才能坐在那裡聽佛說法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、明建立2　天一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明建立，說明所建立的有，分二科；第一科問，提出問題。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何義故建立七有，所謂那落迦、傍生、餓鬼、人、天有，業有，中有？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為什麼要建立這七種有，包括地獄、畜生、餓鬼、人、天有，業有及中有？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、答2　地一、略標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科略標，要略的標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="11679:7144"></a>答：依三種所作故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：是依有情三種所作的原因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、配釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科配釋，配合解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、能引有，謂一；二、趣有有，謂一；三、受用果有，謂五。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七種有分成三類：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、能引有，所造作的業力能夠引發一切果報體的有，由此建立業有。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、趣有有，趣向生有的有，就是中有。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、受用果有，受用五趣果報的有，是指五趣，包括那落迦、傍生、餓鬼、人、天。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p730"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》依三種所作等者：業能引有，是名業有所作。中有趣有，是名中有所作。那落迦等為受用果，是名那落迦等五有所作。依此三種所作差別，建立那落迦等七有應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所造業能引發有，稱為業有所作。中有趣向生有，稱為中有所作。那落迦等五趣的果報體是在該趣的受用果，稱為那落迦等五有所作。依這三種所作的差別，而建立那落迦等七種有應該知道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌十一、生差別2　亥一、別辨相10　天一、生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十一科生差別，生的差別相，分二科；第一科別辨相，各別辨明生的相狀，又分十科；第一科生，說明生的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="6821:7150"></a>生云何？謂於胎、卵二生，初託生時。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　生是什麼？是指胎生和卵生，這二種生命體最初寄託在母腹受生時。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、等生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科等生，說明等生的相狀，等是圓滿的意思。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="39195:7152"></a>等生云何？謂即於彼身分圓滿，仍未出時。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　等生是什麼？是指在母腹的眾生，身分圓滿，身體各部分六根已經圓滿，但還沒有生出的時候。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、趣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科趣，說明趣的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">趣云何？謂從彼出。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　趣是什麼？是指從母腹出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天四、起</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科起，說明起的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">起云何？謂出已增長。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　起是什麼？是指生出來以後，身分逐漸增長。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天五、出現</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科出現，說明出現的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">出現云何？謂於濕、化二生，身分頓起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　出現是什麼？有兩種生命體稱作出現，一種是濕生，一種是化生。濕化二生的身體都是忽然現前，不過他們有差別；化生的人，身體是忽然生出來，六根頓生全部具足；但是濕生，牠的諸根是慢慢生起的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p731"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》生等生趣起者：若諸有情託母胎生，或託卵生，彼初託位名之為生。諸根依處圓滿成就，若未從彼胎、卵出時，是名等生，由遍滿義是等義故。若從彼出，是名為趣，剖胎破殼正趣生故。出已增長，是名為起；謂從嬰孩、童子等位，乃至往趣衰老等位，皆此攝故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果諸多有情是託母胎而生，或是託卵而生，在初託位時稱為生。諸根以及諸根的依處扶根塵，都已經圓滿成就，若是還在母胎或是在卵裡沒有出生，稱為等生，因為諸根及根身都普遍生長圓滿是等的意思。如果從母腹出來，稱為趣，這是由於剖胎或破殼而出，正趣向生時。出生以後繼續長大，稱為起。起，是指從嬰孩、童子等位，乃至往趣衰老等位，都可以稱為起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天六、蘊得</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科蘊得，說明蘊得的相狀，指五蘊成就。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="64334:7162"></a>蘊得云何？謂即於彼諸生位中五取蘊轉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　蘊得是什麼？蘊是積聚的意思，得是成就，蘊得是指前面說的生、等生、趣、起、出現等生位的各種漸次中有五蘊生起活動。轉就是現前或是出現的意思。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天七、界得</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科界得，說明界得的相狀，通常界是指因或者是種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">界得云何？謂即彼諸蘊因緣所攝性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　界得是什麼？界指因，五蘊是由阿賴耶識的業種子及名言種子由愛取滋潤所生，稱為因緣所攝性。由種子產生功能，稱為界得，主要說明生起五蘊的因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天八、處得</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科處得，說明處得的相狀，指六根成就。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">處得云何？謂即彼諸蘊餘緣所攝性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　處得是什麼？五蘊為等無間緣、所緣緣、和增上緣和合而有，稱為餘緣所攝性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷56，1860頁說：為欲顯示等無間緣、所緣緣、增上緣，三種緣義故，建立處得。就是眼耳鼻舌身意六處，六處有心法有色法。有了界得的種子為因緣而有五蘊，五蘊生起之後攝藏於阿賴耶識中的諸根種子，加上等無間緣、所緣緣、增上緣而有處得，諸根才能生起運轉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天九、諸蘊生起</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科諸蘊生起，說明諸蘊生起的相狀，指五蘊相續。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">諸蘊生起云何？謂即彼諸蘊日日飲食之所資長。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　諸蘊生起是什麼？是指五蘊每天必須有段食，觸食，意思食，和識食四種食物來資助長養，才能相續存活。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天十、命根出現</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科命根出現，說明命根出現的相狀，指生命依業力相續。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p732"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">命根出現云何？謂即彼諸蘊餘壽力故，得相續住。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　命根出現是什麼？是指五蘊依業力持續所得的壽命之力，使五蘊得以相續安住。壽力就是命根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》蘊得界得處得者：得有三種，一、種子成就，二、自在成就，三、現行成就。如下決擇分釋。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/52.htm#7172:40441">陵本五十二卷九頁4174</a>）今約現行成就，說名蘊得；種子成就，說名界得；自在成就，說名處得。其義應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　得有三種，包括：一、種子成就，二、自在成就，三、現行成就。如下〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷52，1731頁所解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　現在說現行成就，稱為蘊得；種子成就，稱為界得，自在成就，稱為處得。其中的義理應當了知。五蘊現行，是現行成就；由種子成就五蘊，是界得；由三種緣增上，使六處自在成就是處得。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、結略義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結略義，結說要略的義理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此生支略義者，謂若生自性、若生處位、若所生、若因緣所攝、若任持所引、若俱生依持，是名略義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處所說的生支的要義，是指生的自性─生的特性（生及出現）、生處位─生的過程（等生、趣、起）、所生─所生果（蘊得）、因緣所攝─四緣所攝法（界得、處得）、任持所引─四食任持（諸蘊生起）、俱生依持─命根，是名要略的義理。以下《披尋記》依前文分別再作歸納。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此生支略義等者：生自性攝生及出現；生處位攝等生、趣、起；所生，謂蘊得；若因緣所攝，謂界得、處得；任持所引，謂諸蘊生起；俱生依持，謂命根出現；是名生支略義差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依前文所說，生的自性，含攝生、出現，指胎生與卵生生命體剛託生時及濕化二生的身體頓生；生處位，含攝等生、趣、起，指在母腹時，身分圓滿尚未出生的等生、從母腹出生的趣、出生已後身分逐漸增長的起；所生，是指蘊得的五蘊生起活動；因緣所攝，是指界得、處得（餘三緣），即諸蘊的種子因緣與及生起諸識的增上緣、所緣緣、等無間緣；任持所引，是指諸蘊生起，由四食滋長，使五蘊相續；俱生依持，是指命根出現，依業力持續壽命，使五蘊得以相續安住。以上名為生支的略義差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌十二、老死差別2　亥一、老差別2　天一、別辨相17　地一、衰</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十二科老死差別，說明老差別與死差別，分二科；第一科老差別，說明老的差別，又分二科；第一科別辨相，各別說明老的相狀，又分十七科；第一科衰，說明衰的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="49134:7177"></a>衰云何？謂依止劣故，令彼掉動。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　衰是什麼？指所依止的六根都很下劣，軟弱無力，使六根顫掉，搖搖欲墜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、老</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科老，說明老的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p733"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">老云何？謂髮色衰變。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　老是什麼？指頭髮色變白衰退的變化。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《阿毘達磨大毘婆沙論》卷39說：老與少壯有些不同，頭上開始生出白髮，就是老的開始；若身中增益的大種多、損減的大種少的人，不生白髮。若損減的大種多、增益的大種少的人，頭生白髮；氣勢強的人，不生白髮，氣勢弱的人，頭生白髮；白髮不由老相故起，但眾同分將欲盡時，有此異熟可厭相起。如酒和油等將欲盡時，法爾於中有殘滓汙穢生起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界有情有白髮，色無色界有情沒有，地獄有情沒有白髮，傍生及鬼有；四大洲中除北俱盧洲的人沒有白髮，其餘三洲人有。凡夫聖人都有白髮，諸聖者中從預流果乃至獨覺都有白髮唯除世尊，佛沒有這種可厭相。諸佛都沒有髮希、髮白、皮緩、皮皺、音聲破壞、解支節苦，也沒有心亂漸捨諸根，般涅槃時諸根頓滅。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地三、襵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科襵（音：摺），說明襵的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">襵云何？謂皮膚緩皺。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　襵是什麼？指皮膚鬆弛皺紋增多。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地四、熟</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科熟，說明熟的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">熟云何？謂火力衰減，無復勢力受用欲塵。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　熟是什麼？指身體所有的器官、體能、精神、氣力、飲食都在衰退及遲緩，吃不下、坐不住、站不久、睡不著，再也沒有力能受用種種色聲香味觸的欲塵。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地五、氣力損壞</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科氣力損壞，說明氣力損壞的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">氣力損壞云何？謂性多疾病故，無有勢力能作事業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　氣力損壞是什麼？老的時候，很多疾病都出來了，常常要去看醫生，沒有力量做種種事，有時連端一碗飯、倒一杯水的力量都沒有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地六、黑黶間身</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科黑黶間身，說明黑黶間身的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黑黶間身云何？謂黯黑出現，損其容色。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　黑黶間身是什麼？指臉上、手上、身上開始有黑色的斑點，損害原本潔淨的容貌色相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地七、身脊傴曲喘息奔急</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科身脊傴曲喘息奔急，說明身脊傴曲喘息奔急的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">身脊傴曲、喘息奔急云何？謂行步威儀身形所顯，由此發起極重喘嗽。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　身脊傴曲、喘息奔急是什麼？這是指走路的身形姿態，彎腰駝背，手腿顫動、不穩的樣子，由此引發很重的喘息及咳嗽。傴就是彎腰駝背，走不到幾步就開始喘，步履短而略顯急促，深恐跌倒的樣子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂行步威儀身形所顯者：身脊傴曲，此由身形所顯。喘息奔急，此由行步威儀所顯。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　身體脊椎彎腰駝背，這是由身形所顯現的狀態。喘息奔急，是由行步威儀姿態所顯。走路時很容易喘，是有點老了，如果還不會是還沒有全部老化。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p734"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地八、形貌僂前</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科形貌僂前，說明形貌僂前的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">形貌僂前云何？謂坐威儀位，身首低曲。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　形貌僂前是什麼？是指坐著的時候，頭一直往下垂抬不起來，身體也是彎腰駝背，僂是駝背。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地九、憑據杖策</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科憑據杖策，說明憑據杖策的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">憑據杖策云何？謂住威儀位，依杖力而住。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　憑據杖策是什麼？指住的威儀，是站立時必須要拿柺杖，以支撐腿力與不穩的身體。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地十、昏昧</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科昏昧，說明昏昧的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">昏昧云何？謂臥威儀位，數重睡眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　昏昧是什麼？是指躺臥時的威儀，由於精神不濟，常會昏沉，常常需要睡覺</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地十一、羸劣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十一科羸劣，說明羸劣的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">羸劣云何？謂即於此位，無力速覺。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　羸劣是什麼？是指在這種位階，睡得很沈重，沒有辦法很快醒過來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地十二、損減</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十二科損減，說明損減的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">損減云何？謂念慧衰退。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　損減是什麼？是指記憶力及智慧的觀察、決擇力衰退。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地十三、衰退</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十三科衰退，說明衰退的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">衰退云何？謂念慧劣故，至於善法不能現行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　衰退是什麼？是指念力與思惟決擇的慧力退失而羸劣，導致於想要修行的善法退失不能現行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》衰退云何等者：由念慧劣，是故名衰。由信等善法不能現行於前，是故名退。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　念力與智慧都慢慢的衰弱了，是名為衰。由此信進念定慧這些善法都不能現行，因此說名為退。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p735"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地十四、諸根耄熟</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十四科諸根耄熟，說明諸根耄熟的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">諸根耄熟云何？謂身體尫羸。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　諸根耄熟是什麼？是指六根功能衰退，身體非常虛弱羸劣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地十五、功用破壞</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十五科功用破壞，說明功用破壞的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">功用破壞云何？謂彼於境不復明利。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　功用破壞是什麼？在眼耳鼻舌身意接觸色聲香味觸法時，諸根的功能已經衰退到破壞，沒有那麼清楚俐落了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　例如眼睛本來沒有老花眼的，現在慢慢有老花眼了，耳朵本來沒有重聽的，現在慢慢聽不到，鼻子也不大靈，吃東西沒有胃口，身體不是那麼俐落，站起來坐下來都要花很久的時間，記憶力及智慧等都衰退。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地十六、諸行朽故</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十六科諸行朽故，說明諸行朽故的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="64353:7212"></a>諸行朽故云何？謂彼於後將欲終時。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　諸行朽故是什麼？指眼耳口鼻舌身意諸根及五蘊已經枯朽衰竭，快要臨命終時。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地十七、其形腐敗</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十七科其形腐敗，說明其形腐敗的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">其形腐敗云何？謂壽量將盡，身形臨壞，於諸事業無復功能。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其形腐敗是什麼？這時已經接近死亡，壽量將盡，四大快要敗壞，對於任何事情都沒有能力去做了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、結略義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結略義，結說要略的義理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="40368:7216"></a>此老略義者，謂依止變壞、鬚髮變壞、充悅變壞、火力變壞、無病變壞、色相變壞、威儀變壞、無色諸根變壞、有色諸根變壞、時分已過、壽量將盡，略義應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此中十七句老的要義可歸納成十一種，是指依止變壞─六根衰退；鬚髮變壞─髮色衰變；充悅變壞─皮膚緩皺；火力變壞─火力衰減，無復勢力受用欲塵；無病變壞─性多疾病故，無有勢力能作事業；色相變壞─黑黶間身；威儀變壞─身脊傴曲喘息奔急及形貌僂前與憑據杖策；無色諸根變壞─昏昧、羸劣、損減、衰退；有色諸根變壞─諸根耄熟與功用破壞；時分已過─諸行朽故；壽量將盡─其形腐敗，其中要略的義理應該要知道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p736"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此老略義等者：老支差別，前文別釋有十七句，今結略義總有十一。依止變壞等，別配差別中初六句；威儀變壞攝差別中次五句；無色諸根變壞攝差別中第十二、十三兩句；有色諸根變壞攝差別中第十四、十五兩句；時分已過、壽量將盡別配差別中第十六、十七兩句應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　老支的差別，將前文各別解釋有十七句，現在結要義歸納成十一句。依止變壞等，指身體各部分衰退的情形，各別配十七句差別中初六句，包括衰、老、襵、熟、氣力損壞及黑黯間身等；威儀變壞，指行住坐臥四威儀也會開始有變壞，攝十七句差別中次五句，包括身脊傴曲喘息奔急、形貌僂前、憑據杖策、昏昧、羸劣等。無色諸根變壞，指念慧衰退於善法不能現行等，攝差十七句差別中第十二、十三兩句的損減與衰退。有色諸根變壞，指眼等五根衰退，攝差十七句差別中第十四、十五兩句的諸根耄熟、功用破壞。時分已過、壽量將盡，各別配十七句差別中的第十六、十七兩句的諸行朽故、其形腐敗。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、死差別2　天一、約補特伽羅相辨2　地一、彼彼有情</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科死差別，死的差別，分二科；第一科約補特伽羅相辨，約人的相貌來說，又分二科；第一科彼彼有情，說明各種有情的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼彼有情云何？謂那落迦等有情。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　彼彼有情是什麼？是指地獄、餓鬼、畜生、人、及天等三界有情。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、種類</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科種類，有情的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">種類云何？謂即彼一切。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有情的種類是什麼？指三界五趣中，每一趣都有各式各樣的有情，死的情況都不一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂即彼一切者：彼謂那落迦等彼彼有情，於中復有眾多差別，是名一切。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡所說的「彼」是指地獄、餓鬼、畜生、人、天等五趣的種種有情，每一趣中的有情又有很多的差別，因此名為一切。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、約法相辨2　地一、別辨相9　玄一、終</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約法相辨，約死的法相說明，分二科；第一科別辨相，各別說明死的相狀，又分九科；第一科終，說明終的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">終云何？謂諸有情離解支節而死。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　終是什麼？是指諸有情遠離解支節的苦而死。〈五識身相應地〉卷1，37頁說，天人及那落迦有情是化生的，沒有解支節的苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、盡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科盡，說明盡的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">盡云何？謂諸有情由解支節而死。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　盡是什麼？是指諸有情是由解支節而死。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　人將命終時，有風氣，解支節如刀，稱為刀風，又名解支節，能將皮肉筋骨脂髓精血一切解截。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《五王經》說：「欲死時刀風解形，無處不痛。」《安樂集》上說：「若刀風一至，百苦輳身。」《行事鈔資持記》上一之下說：「能解支節故喻如刀。」除了天人及那落迦有情是化生的，沒有解支節的苦，其餘欲界有情都有解支節苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p737"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》離解支節及解支節而死者：天、那落迦，離解支節而死。所餘生處，解支節死。如前意地已說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/01.htm#7229:646">陵本一卷十五頁77</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　天與那落迦是化生的，沒有解支節苦，離解支節而死。欲界其他處所受生有情，將命終時，身體中皮肉筋骨脂髓精血等被風大割截分解，像烏龜脫殼一樣痛苦。如〈意地〉卷1，37頁已說過。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄三、壞</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科壞，說明壞的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壞云何？謂識離身。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　壞是什麼？是指阿賴耶識捨離身體。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂識離身者：識捨所依，名識離身。或從上捨，或從下捨，如是最後乃至心處。如前意地已說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/01.htm#7232:661">陵本一卷十六頁79</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　阿賴耶識捨離所依止的色身，名為識離身。識捨離身時或是從上方頭部往下捨離，或是從下方腳部往上捨離，這樣最後漸漸到心臟處捨離身體。如前〈意地〉卷1，38頁已說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄四、沒</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科沒，說明沒（音：歿）的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">沒云何？謂諸色根滅。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　沒是什麼？是指眼耳鼻舌身諸根滅壞。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂諸色根滅者：五有色根最後滅已，不更相續故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　諸色根滅指五種有色根最後滅壞之後，不能繼續使用，眼不能見乃至身不能感觸，稱為沒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄五、捨壽</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科捨壽，說明捨壽的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">捨壽云何？謂氣將盡位。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　捨壽是什麼？是指氣息將要完全耗盡時。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄六、捨煖</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科捨煖，說明捨煖的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">捨煖云何？謂不動位。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　捨煖是什麼？是指肢體不能動了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p738"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂不動位者：由捨煖已，身僵仆故，不能運轉，得不動名。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不動位，是指捨煖以後，身體僵直，不能再動了，因此稱為不動。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄七、棄捨諸蘊命根謝滅</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科棄捨諸蘊命根謝滅，說明棄捨諸蘊命根謝滅的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="53001:7243"></a>棄捨諸蘊命根謝滅云何？謂時死。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　棄捨諸蘊命根謝滅是什麼？是指壽盡故死。例如這人的壽命本來是一百歲，一百歲時才死，稱為棄捨諸蘊命根謝滅。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄八、死</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科死，說明死的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">死云何？謂遇橫緣，非時而死。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　死是什麼？是指遇到橫緣，不是應該死的時候而死。橫緣，是非時死的橫死因緣而死，並非由前世之業果而導致命終。《藥師經》說橫死有：得病無醫、王法誅戮、非人奪取精氣、火焚、水溺、惡獸啗、墮崖、毒藥咒咀、飢渴所困，共九種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂時死非時死者：隨感壽量滿盡故死，此名時死。若由福盡，或不避不平等故死，名非時死。如前意地已說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/01.htm#7246:536">陵本一卷十三頁65</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有情隨過去生感得的壽量已經圓滿、受用盡了，稱為時死。若是由於福報盡了或不避不平等而死，稱為非時死。如前〈意地〉卷1，32～34頁已說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄九、時蘊盡2　黃一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科時蘊盡，說明時蘊盡的相狀，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">時蘊盡云何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　時蘊盡是什麼？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、釋2　宇一、第一義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科第一義，說明時蘊盡第一種相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂初死未久位。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　剛死不久時，稱為時蘊盡。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇二、第二義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二義，說明時蘊盡的第二種相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又死魔業名時蘊盡。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或者說死魔業名為時蘊盡。人壽盡命終為魔，因為業報已盡，捨離現生之處，障蔽修道，喪失智慧之命，因此稱為死魔。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p739"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》時蘊盡等者：一期五蘊夭喪殞歿，不相續住，名時蘊盡。當知此是死魔所作，由五取蘊現在生已，便有夭喪殞歿隨逐故，是故死魔業亦名時蘊盡。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一期生命體的五蘊壽力已盡，死亡殞歿，不再相續安住，名為時蘊盡。應當知道這是由死魔所作，只要由五取蘊現在生了以後，便會有夭折喪亡殞歿隨逐，因此死魔業也名為時蘊盡。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、結略義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結略義，結說要略的義理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此死略義者，謂若死、若死法、若死差別、若死後位，是名略義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡所說死的要略義理，是指死─終與盡；死法─壞與沒；死差別─捨壽、捨煖、棄捨諸蘊命根謝滅、死、時蘊盡；死後位─時蘊盡，這些稱為略義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此死略義等者：於中若死攝初二句，若死法攝次二句，若死差別攝次六句，若死後位結後一句應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在其中若死含攝初二句的終與盡，若死法含攝次二句的壞與沒，若死差別所攝次六句的捨壽、捨煖、棄捨諸蘊命根謝滅、死、及時蘊盡的二種義，若死後位結後一句的時蘊盡應該知道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結說緣起差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是名為緣起差別應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說稱為緣起差別應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未五、緣起次第難2　申一、別辨3　酉一、順次第說2　戌一、問難</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科緣起次第難，對於緣起次第的難問，分二科；第一科別辨，各別的說明，又分三科；第一科順次第說，解釋順次第說的難問，又分二科；第一科問難，難問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何因緣故，無明等諸有支作如是次第說？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：是什麼因緣，無明等諸有支要以無明緣行，行緣識乃至生緣老死的次第來說？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、答釋3　亥一、第一差別2　天一、釋10　地一、無明緣行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答釋，回答解釋，依順次第分為三種說明，分三科；第一科第一差別，說明第一種差別，又分二科；第一科釋，解釋，又分十科；第一科無明緣行，說明無明緣行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：諸愚癡者要先愚於所應知事，次即於彼發起邪行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：愚癡就是有無明的人，所有愚癡沒有智慧的人，要先愚昧於所應知的緣生諸法，於緣生法不知唯有如幻諸行，妄起我見及我慢我執等，其次為自受樂或非苦樂故，對於所愚癡的緣生諸法，造作福行、非福行、和不動行等能夠引生三界苦果的邪行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這一段文意指無明緣行，無明是指於隨順假名安立的一切法執為實有的心，依此執為我我所，因此顛倒心能集聚造作諸業，稱為無明緣行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p740"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》諸愚癡者至發起邪行者：謂現法中，名色為緣六處生起，是名所應知事。不斷不知，故名為愚。由是六處名為無明引因依處。如下決擇分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/56.htm#7265:44729">陵本五十六卷十六頁4545</a>）福與非福及不動行皆名邪行，能引苦故，非解脫故。</span></strong></span></span></p>
