<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有情入母胎所得的生命體稱為名色。在現法中，以名色為緣，慢慢長出六根等，是名所應知事。對所應認識的生命體的形成與死生流轉這件事，不能斷除這種苦果的一再生起與流轉，也不明白能感得果報體的種種原因，因此稱為愚。眼等六處是無明引因的依止處，由六根接觸六境而有種種的愚癡生起，稱為無明引因依處。如下〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷56，1862頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五戒十善等福行、五逆、十惡等非福行、修世間禪定，報生色界、無色界天等不動行，都是不能出離三界含有顛倒的邪行，能夠引生苦果，不是真實的解脫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、行緣識</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科行緣識，說明行緣識。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由邪行故，令心顛倒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由福行、非福行及不動行等邪行熏成隨業識，此識隨順所造業行，令中有心生顛倒，馳赴所生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地三、識緣名色</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科識緣名色，說明識緣名色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">心顛倒故，結生相續。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於中有心生顛倒，於當生父母所出濃厚精血、合成一段，此時中有滅；與滅同時，即由一切種子識功能力故，有餘微細根及大種和合而生，及餘有根同分精血和合摶生。於此時中，說識已住，結生相續，即此名為羯羅藍位。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地四、名色緣六處</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科名色緣六處，說明名色緣六處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">生相續故，諸根圓滿。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　結生相續，生命相續之後，眼等六根逐漸成熟圓滿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地五、六處緣觸觸緣受</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科六處緣觸觸緣受，說明六處緣觸、觸緣受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">根圓滿故，二受用境。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　諸根圓滿後，與境和合便有識生，根與識二種便能受用境界；由根境識三和故有順樂受等觸生，依此便生樂等三受。從此三受引生三愛：由苦逼有情於樂受發生欲愛，或有於樂非苦樂受發生色愛，或有唯於非苦樂受生無色愛。從欣受愛起欲等取，受用色聲香味觸法六塵。這是說明六處圓滿而有觸，由觸根與識便能受用境。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地六、受緣愛</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科受緣愛，說明受緣愛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">受用境故，若耽著，若希求。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從此三受引生三愛，於五妙欲境之樂受發生欲愛，或有於樂受、非苦樂受發生色愛，或有唯於非苦樂受生無色愛。由此耽著從五欲，或於色無色定生起染污希求。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p741"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地七、愛緣取</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科愛緣取，說明愛緣取。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由希求故，於方覓時煩惱滋長。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由染污希求三界愛，在希求尋覓所愛境時，貪愛的煩惱增長而生起欲等取。欲取是指於欲界色聲香味觸五塵之境，貪欲取著；見取是指取著於六十二見等之邪心分別；戒禁取，依於邪見取著錯誤的身語，謬以為戒，由此成行，如外道持雞狗等戒；我語取，於五蘊隨假言說取著於我，生我、我見、我慢等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地八、取緣有</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科取緣有，說明取緣有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="7657:7280"></a>煩惱滋長故，發起後有愛非愛業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於煩惱不斷的增長為緣，使前生所熏成的行乃至識、名色、六處、觸、受，六法的種子變成為有，就會發起招感後有可愛的或不可愛的果報。在欲、色界此時的有仍是種子的狀態。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》發起後有愛非愛業者：謂令先所引發愛非愛業，從此命終漸生起故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於愛、取滋潤形成強而有力的增上緣，使令過去所造的善非善業行的種子被引發成有，從此生命終後，以有為緣，識相續流轉趣向未來受生，欲界可愛的人身或餓鬼處畜生等不可愛的果報就逐漸生起。漸生是指欲界胎卵二生有情。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地九、有緣生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科有緣生，說明有緣生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由所起業滋長力故，於五趣生死中苦果生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於所造的業行，由愛、取的滋養增長達到「有」的力量，在五趣生死中即會有種種的苦果生起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地十、生緣老死2　玄一、標說</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科生緣老死，說明生緣老死，有生就會有老死，分二科；第一科標說，標出說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">苦果生已，有老死等苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五趣的異熟苦果已經生出，一定會有老病死等苦隨逐。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、釋苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋苦，解釋苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂內身變異所引老死苦，及境界變異所引憂歎苦熱惱之苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　苦是指由內身變異所引生的老病死苦，及境界變異所引生的憂愁、感嘆、苦惱、熱惱等擾亂自己內心的種種苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結語第一種由無明所引發的次第說十二支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故世尊如是次第說十二支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此世尊依這樣的次第說十二有支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p742"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》境界變異所引憂歎苦熱惱者：此所引苦，餘處說名愁、歎、苦、憂、惱。由可愛事無常轉變，悲傷心慼，故名為愁。由彼發言咨嗟歔欷，故名為歎。因此拊膺，故名為苦。內懷冤結，故名為憂。因茲迷亂，故名為惱。復有餘釋，如下攝事分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/88.htm#7291:67155">陵本八十八卷三頁6644</a>）今此所說，次第少異，然義無別，故應準釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由境界變異所引的苦，其他的經典說為愁、歎、苦、憂、惱。由於可愛的事情無常轉變，感覺悲傷心慼，因此說名為愁。由於憂愁發出歎息悲痛哭泣的聲音，故名為歎。因此自己拍打自己的胸，故名為苦。內心懷著冤苦煩惱，故名為憂。由於有愁歎苦憂而迷惑惱亂，故名為惱。如下〈攝事分〉卷88，2615頁所說。現在所說的次第稍有不同，但義理沒有什麼差別，所以應該準照〈攝事分〉解釋。這是第一種差別，說到無明緣行乃至生緣老死，為什麼要依這種次第說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、第二差別4　天一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二差別，說明第二種差別，分四科；第一科標，標出差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有次第差別，謂依二種緣建立緣起次第。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次又有次第差別，是指依止二種緣來建立十二緣起的次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、內身緣，二、受用境界緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、內身緣，指由無明的業行所熏習的內身種子的緣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、受用境界緣，領受享用色聲香味觸法的境界緣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依著內身與受用境界這二種緣來安立十二緣起的次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科攝，說明十二支所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">內身緣，前六支所攝；受用境界緣，後六支所攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　內身緣，是十二有支中前六支所攝；受用境界緣，是十二有支中後六支所攝。為什麼要這樣說？無明緣行乃至觸這前六支是招感當來內身的緣，從受緣愛乃至生緣老死後六支，由受用境界生起愛取而感果。因此依據這兩種道理，這樣安立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天四、釋2　地一、由內身緣2　玄一、能引支攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科由內身緣，說明由內身緣，又分二科；第一科能引支攝，說明能引支所攝，無明緣行，行緣識。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p743"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">先於內身起我執等愚，由此不了諸業所引苦果異熟故，發起諸業。既發起已，即隨彼業多起尋思。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於有情對自己的身心生起各式各樣的我執等愚癡，因此不明白所造作的福業、非福業、或不動業所引生異熟的苦果，又造作種種的福業、非福業、或不動業。既發不動業行以後，就隨著自己造的業生起種種的分別尋思。這是由無明引發造業，由業行造作時，同時熏習到阿賴耶識中。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》即隨彼業多起尋思者：謂隨彼彼諸所作業，由不如理作意所引，妄起分別尋思行故，如十六異論諸差別是。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在前面〈有尋有伺等三地〉卷6與卷7說過隨種種有情所造的業，是由不如理作意所引發的，造業後又繼續虛妄分別、尋思，就會有種種不同的思想理論產生，如十六異論等不同的邪論。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、所引支攝3　黃一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科所引支攝，說明所引支所攝，分三科；第一科標，標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由業與識為助伴故，能感當來三種苦果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面說無明所引造了業行，於識中熏成種子，由於業種子與識種子等為助伴的緣故，能感得下一生的三種苦果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂根初起所攝苦果、根圓滿所攝苦果、受用境界所攝苦果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　下一生的三種苦果，是指識入母胎六根剛剛生起所攝的苦果就是名色；六根圓滿時所攝苦果就是六處位；有了六處就可受用境界所攝苦果，就是觸，這三種稱為三種苦果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即名色為先，觸為最後。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這就是識緣名色、名色緣六處，六處緣觸。這是所引支，包括名色、六處、觸，觸是最後一支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、由受用境界緣2　玄一、能生支攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由受用境界緣，說明由受用境界緣，分二科；第一科能生支攝，說明能生支所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於現法中，依觸緣受，發起於愛。由受用境界緣廣起追求，或由事業門，或由利養門，或由戒禁門，或由解脫門，發起欲求、內身求、邪解脫求。如是求時，令先所起煩惱及業所引五趣生死果生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在現在的生命體的受想行識中，依觸緣受，有感受而發起愛煩惱。由受用境界緣而廣泛的追求，或由事業門或由利養門發起欲求，或由戒禁門發起內身求，或由解脫門發起邪解脫求。於這樣追求時，能使令先所生起的煩惱及業所引發的五趣生死苦果生起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是由受緣愛，愛緣取時，取緣有的能生支，可使過去無明及業所引生的識乃至受五法的種子現行，到五趣中受生死苦果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p744"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、所生支攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科所生支攝，說名所生支所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">既得生已，老死隨逐。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　既得到生以後，老死必然隨逐。生就是識、名色、六處、觸、受的現行，現行以後就會有老死了。這是第二種差別，約內身緣和受用境界緣來說十二緣起的次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》或由事業門等者：如前已說四所為取，今此四門如次別配，其義可知。由前二門發起欲求；由戒禁門發起有求，即內身求；由解脫門發起邪解脫求。欲等三求，如前有尋有伺地說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/05.htm#7313:3390">陵本五卷七頁342</a>）此中道理，隨應當釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前已說事業門、利養門、戒禁門、解脫門四門是所為取，現在這裡四門如其次第各別配合解釋所求，其中的義理可以知道。由前二門的事業門與利養門發起欲求；由戒禁門發起有求，即內身求；由解脫門發起邪解脫求。欲求、內身求、邪解脫求這三求，如前〈有尋有伺地〉卷5，137頁中所說，此中的道理，隨所對應的應當如此解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是第二種道理，由內身緣和受用境緣來安立十二緣起的次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、第三差別2　天一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科第三差別，十二支次第安立的第三種差別，分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有次第差別，謂由三種有情聚。一、樂出世清淨，二、樂世間清淨，三、樂著境界。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有次第差別，由三種有情聚，一、愛樂出世間無漏清淨者，二、愛樂世間離欲清淨者，三、愛樂執著諸欲境界者，有這三種差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、隨釋3　地一、由初有情聚</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋，分三科；第一科由初有情聚，說明第一類有情聚，指愛樂出世間無漏清淨有情類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由初聚故，滅諸緣起，增白淨品。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種愛樂出世間無漏清淨有情，是指修學佛法聖道的人，由修習戒定慧，斷滅生死流轉十二緣起諸支，增長白淨善法類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、由第二有情聚2　玄一、初三支攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由第二有情聚，說明第二類有情聚，分二科；第一科初三支攝，說明初三支無明、行、識所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p745"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由第二有情聚故，不如實知諸諦道理。若住正念，或作福業，或作有漏修所引不動業；若不住正念，便發非福業。或起追悔所引，或不追悔歡喜所引心相續住。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種愛樂世間離欲清淨有情之類，追求離欲的世間清淨，但是不能如實知道四諦的道理。如果安住正念，能持戒布施造作福業，或者是造作有漏修行所引生的禪定等不動業；如果不安住在正念中，就會造作非福的惡業。或生起追悔所造作的惡業，或是不追悔所造的福及不動業，由歡喜所引，使心相續而住。這是第二類的人。好一點，但是還是在輪迴中。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》或起追悔所引等者：此說二種心相續住。謂發非福業者，便起追悔所引心相續住，由非福業惡作罪聚攝故。若作福業、或不動業，便起不追悔歡喜所引心相續住。聲聞地說：先於尸羅善清淨故，便無憂悔；無憂悔故，歡喜安樂；由有樂故，心得正定。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/28.htm#7321:23206">陵本二十八卷二頁2327</a>）此中道理，應如是知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是說二種心相續住，是指造作非福業的人，就會生起後悔所引令心相續而住，因為非福業是惡作罪聚所攝。如果造作福業、或不動業，就不會追悔，由歡喜所引令心相續而住，由此容易得定。〈聲聞地〉說要先持戒清淨，就不會有憂愁後悔；沒有憂愁後悔就能令心歡喜安樂；因為歡喜安樂，心能夠成就正定。如〈聲聞地〉卷28，940頁所說，此處道理，應準照那裡所說而知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、次三支攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科次三支攝，說明次三支名色、六處、觸三支所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼又如前，於下中上生處，次第能感當來三種苦果，謂名色為先，觸為最後。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種有情如前所說，由於所造的福業、非福業、不動業，在下品的欲界、中品的色界、上品的無色界，依次第能感得未來的根初起、根圓滿、受用境界三種異熟的苦果，即名色為先，觸為最後的名色緣六處，六處緣觸，名色、六處、觸三支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》彼又如前於下中上生處等者：此中彼言，謂第二有情聚。或求欲生，或求樂生，各有三種生處差別，謂下中上。有尋有伺地中已說其相。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/05.htm#7324:3353">陵本五卷六頁339</a>）於彼彼處，依內身緣能感當來三種苦果。謂根初起所攝苦果、根圓滿所攝苦果、受用境界所攝苦果。此三差別，前文已說，故指如前。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡所說的彼，是指第二種有情類。這類有情或是追求欲界的欲樂，或是追求色界的禪定樂，各有三種生處的差別，包括下中上三品。下品欲界即三種欲生，第一種欲生，現住欲塵，由此現住欲塵故，富貴自在，包括一切人、四大王眾天乃至知足天；第二種欲生，變化欲塵，由此變化欲塵故，富貴自在，如樂化天；第三種欲生，他化欲塵，由他所化諸欲塵故，富貴自在，即他化自在天；及中品色界三種樂生，第一種樂生指初禪，第二種樂生指二禪，第三種樂生指三禪。如〈有尋有伺地〉卷5，136頁中已詳細說明其中的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在各種不同的處所，依內身緣能招感當來三種苦果，包括根初起所攝苦果就是名色，根圓滿所攝苦果是六處，受用境界所攝苦果是觸。這三處的三種差別，如前文已經說過，因此指出如前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p746"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地三、由第三有情聚</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科由第三有情聚，說明第三類有情聚。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由第三有情聚故，依現受用境所生受，於現法中如前次第起後六支，謂受為先，老死為後。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於第三種愛樂執著諸欲境界的有情，依止現在受用的境界時所生的感受，在現在的生命體當中依次第生起受、愛、取、有、生、老死後六支，即受為先，老死為後的受緣愛、愛緣取、取緣有、有緣生、生緣老死。這是第三種有情的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上佛陀由順次第說的三種差別：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、由無明諸愚癡者要先愚於所應知事，次即於彼發起邪行，建立緣起次第；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、依內身緣（前六支）及受用境界緣（後六支）二種緣，建立緣起次第；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、由三種有情聚：樂出世清淨、樂世間清淨、樂著境界的不同，來建立緣起次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、逆次第說2　戌一、問難</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科逆次第說，逆次第說十二緣起，分二科；第一科問難，提出問題難問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何因緣故，逆次第中老死為先說諸緣起？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：是什麼因緣，逆次第中要先說老死，然後再說其他的緣起？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、答釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答釋，回答解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依止宣說諦道理故，以生及老死能顯苦諦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：依止諸佛菩薩宣示解說四諦道理的緣故，因為生及老死能夠顯出苦諦，因此先說老死再說生。老死很苦，大家都能夠明白。為什麼會老死？因為有生。生就是苦的開始，所以生及老死可以顯示苦諦。眾生於此深有感受，先這樣說才能應機，引發眾生離苦得樂的出離心。所以佛在《阿含經》中說，如果眾生沒有老病死，他不需要化現在這個世間，因為大家都不喜歡苦。所以要從苦諦開始說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》逆次第中至能顯苦諦者：此中道理，如下攝事分中緣起擇說應知。謂始從老死，次第逆觀苦、集二諦緣起道理故。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/93.htm#7332:71062">陵本九十三卷六頁7004</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這其中的道理，如下〈攝事分〉卷93，2752頁中「緣起擇說」所說應當了知。說到十二緣起。開始從老死次第，逆觀苦集二諦緣起的道理。先觀察老死從哪裡來？從生來；接下來觀察生從哪裡來？從有來；有從哪裡來？從取來；取從哪裡來？從愛來；愛從哪裡來？從受來等，由此先開示苦諦，再開示集諦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、舉異經說2　戌一、引經難</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科舉異經說，舉出經典上有不同的說法，分二科；第一科引經難，引出經典所說來難問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如世尊言：新名色滅為上首法。問：何故不言諸無明滅為上首耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如世尊說：新名色滅是最殊勝的法。問：為什麼不說諸無明滅是最殊勝的法呢？新是對舊來說的，是指相對於今生舊的果報，下一生新的果報，在十二緣起中指生支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p747"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》新名色滅為上首法等者：此舉經問。由前已說，無明滅故，行滅；次第乃至異熟生觸滅故，異熟生受滅。又說，於現法中，無明觸所生受滅故，愛滅，乃至取等惱最為後諸行永滅。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/09.htm#7336:6843">陵本九卷十五頁695</a>）若如是者，何故世尊於餘經中作如是說：新名色滅為上首法？此中問意，如是應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡是舉出經典所說提問。因為前面已經說過，無明滅除以後，行即滅，不會去造三種邪行，依次第，行滅則識滅，識滅則名色滅，名色滅則觸滅，乃至異熟生觸滅，則異熟生受也滅了。又說在現在的生命體當中，由無明觸所生的受滅後，愛也滅，乃至取、有、生、老死憂悲苦惱最後諸行永滅。如〈有尋有伺等三地〉卷9，286頁所說：取滅故有滅，有滅故生滅，生滅故老死滅，稱為取等惱最後諸行永滅。通常經典都說：「無明滅故行滅，乃至愛滅故取滅，取滅故有滅，有滅故生滅，生滅故老死滅」。都是這樣次第說，為什麼佛要開示新名色滅為上首呢？此處提問的意思是這樣，應該知道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、依義答2　亥一、標施設</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依義答，依其中的義理回答，分二科；第一科標施設，標出施設。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依心解脫者而施設故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：這是依心解脫者而施設安立的。無明滅故得到慧解脫，因為將無明滅除，不再有不如理作意，由此心離於貪愛之繫縛，而得解脫，故名心解脫。這是約心解脫的阿羅漢來安立的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋所由2　天一、名色不生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋所由，解釋緣由，分二科；第一科名色不生，說明名色不生的前因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由彼於現法中種子苦及當來苦果不生而滅，故說名色為先，受為最後，得究竟滅。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　心解脫的阿羅漢在現在的生命體當中，由於明相應觸所生受，心已解脫，不會再有新名色的種子熏習下去，即使仍有舊名色的種子，因為三界愛見煩惱已經斷除，種子苦因不會再有愛的增上緣滋潤和合，使將來的苦果不再生起而滅，因此說名色為先，受為最後，得到究竟的寂滅。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、愛隨眠滅</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科愛隨眠滅，愛煩惱種子的滅除。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於現法中受諸受時，愛及隨眠永拔不起說名為滅。由彼滅故，以彼為先餘支亦滅。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又在現在的生命體當中，領納各種樂受、不樂受、不苦不樂受時，心中愛的現行及愛的種子永遠斷除不再生起，稱為滅。由愛滅了，以愛為先其餘取、有、生、老死支也都不起而滅。愛滅故取滅，取滅故有滅，有滅故生一定是滅的，新名色即滅了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是依據心解脫的人來說的，心解脫的人：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、已經斷除無明，不會再造業行，熏成新名色的種子，將來生支的苦果也不會生了；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、現在接觸種種境界的感受，愛取的煩惱種子通通沒有了，也不生煩惱，因此下一生生支也不會再生起，新的生命體也不會出現了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p748"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》依心解脫至餘支亦滅者：此中初句總標經意。謂心解脫諸阿羅漢，於現法中無明及愛永斷無餘，依彼施設新名色滅為上首法，故不更言諸無明滅。餘文隨釋。謂彼心解脫者，於現法中無名色等新種熏習，當來苦果永不更生，由是說言新名色滅。又於現法貪愛永滅，唯餘清淨識緣名色、名色緣識，亦依此說新名色滅。由是後後諸支皆得永滅，依此說彼為上首法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這其中第一句已總相標示出經中所說的要義。因為心解脫的諸阿羅漢，在現在的生命體中無明與愛已永遠斷除，依彼心解脫的諸阿羅漢安立新名色滅為上首法，所以不再說諸無明滅。其他的文隨著解釋。心解脫的人在現在的生命體當中，沒有名色等新的種子熏習，下一生的五蘊苦果永遠不會再生出來，因此說是新名色滅。這是第一種解釋。又由於現在的貪愛永滅，不會再滋潤識中的舊名色種，只剩下清淨的識緣名色、名色緣識，心解脫的阿羅漢五蘊及識現在都是清淨的，也依此說新名色滅。因此後後的取、有、生、老死諸支都得以永遠滅除，依著這個道理，說新名色滅為上首。這當中有二義，一、無明滅，二、愛滅，不用再明說無明滅為上首，因為已包括在裡面。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷3說：現在名色所有種子不生當果。先觀苦諦故，以名色滅為上首。名色滅是由能潤集諦所攝愛取等滅，因此名色等種當來不生果。名色等種是當來世生老死的因緣，屬親因緣故說此名色先滅，無明等屬疏緣的增上緣所攝，逆次第於最後才觀察。無明等是能引及能潤因故，不說無明為先首滅。故證得無學已後，逆觀察由誰無故老死無等。餘次第滅准此應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、總結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科總結，總說結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是等類，宣說緣起次第應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依這三大類，佛陀宣說緣起的次第。第一是順次第說，其中又分成三種差別，第二是逆次第說，第三是舉異經說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未六、緣起釋詞2　申一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科緣起釋詞，解釋緣起的詞義，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何故緣起說為緣起？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：什麼原因將緣起說為緣起？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、答5　酉一、依字釋名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分五科；第一科依字釋名，依緣起的字來解釋它的名義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：由煩惱繫縛，往諸趣中數數生起故，名為緣起。此依字釋名。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：由於煩惱繫縛，一次又一次往五趣中現起新的生命，名為緣起。這是依字解釋名義。緣，是被煩惱繫縛。起，是往諸趣中數數生起生命。總說由於煩惱繫縛到五趣當中數數生起各式各樣的生命體，稱為緣起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由煩惱繫縛等者：此中煩惱繫縛，釋名為緣。往諸趣中數數生起，釋名為起。如是總說十二有支應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這其中依煩惱繫縛，解釋名為緣。往五趣中一次又一次現起新的生命，解釋名為起。這些總說為十二有支應該知道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、依剎那義釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依剎那義釋，依剎那義解釋緣起。緣起的剎那義，能遮止聲聞乘部派中的大眾部和化地部認為緣起是無為，及遮止正量部所說一期有生老住無常四相的說法，而說緣起是剎那生滅，不是一期生滅而已。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，依託眾緣，速謝滅已，續和合生，故名緣起。此依剎那義釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，依託因緣、等無間緣、所緣緣、增上緣的眾緣和合剎那而生，剎那就謝滅了，剎那又相續和合而生，因此名為緣起。這是依剎那義解釋。五蘊是剎那生剎那滅，並不像眼睛所看到的一個整體一直連續下來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p749"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》依託眾緣等者：緣有四種，所謂因緣、等無間緣、所緣緣，并增上緣。諸支生時，色無色行更互為緣，或多或少，義如下說，是名依託眾緣，此釋緣義。生已即滅，滅已續生，此釋起義。當知此義唯依諸緣生法剎那無常為論，非說諸支次第為緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　緣有四種，包括因緣、等無間緣、所緣緣，增上緣。在十二有支諸支次第生起時，色行與無色的心行更相互為緣，或多分或少分，義理如下所說，稱依託眾緣，這是解釋「緣」的義理。生了後剎那即滅，滅了後剎那又相續而生，這是解釋「起」的義理。應當知道這裡的義理只是依止諸緣生法的剎那無常所說的，並不是指諸支的前後次第為緣。若詳細觀察，一剎那已具足十二緣起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、依有作用義釋3　戌一、標義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科依有作用義釋，依有作用義解釋緣起，分三科；第一科標義，標出其中的義理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，眾緣過去而不捨離，依自相續而得生起，故名緣起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，諸緣生法依託眾緣生現行以後，因已受盡，自性已滅，然而在法和合生起的同時，所生法的種子也同時熏習到阿賴耶識當中，因此所生法與眾緣雖謝滅而所熏習的種子在阿賴耶識中並未捨離，雖經百千劫，假使因緣和合，依於自身相續的阿賴耶識中種子仍會生起現行，能令有情的愛非愛果異熟成熟，因此名為緣起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、引證</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科引證，引佛在《雜阿含經》所說證明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如說：此有故彼有，此生故彼生，非餘。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如佛所說：此有故彼有，此生故彼生，由此可知諸法並不是自生、他生、共生、無因而生，或如聲聞乘說由無為而生或如外道說由常法而生。此有故彼有，是說因為有種子，遇緣就有現行產生，現行產生以後，又引發另一現行生出來，而此生故彼生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《法華經玄贊要集》卷29說非餘：是說諸法以無明行為緣，識等果法方有，非如小乘大眾部義，緣生法以「無為」為體，非如外道常法能生一切，因此說「非餘」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、結名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結名，結說依有作用義釋名。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依此義故，釋名應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依此有作用義的道理來解釋緣起的名字，應該要了解。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p750"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》眾緣過去而不捨離等者：諸緣生法依託眾緣生現行已，因已受盡，自性已滅。然彼無間熏習相續有種子生，雖經久劫，猶能令彼愛非愛果異熟當熟，是即因性名為緣起。緣起經說：此有故彼有，此生故彼生。當知謂此無明隨眠不斷有故，彼無明纏有；此無明纏生故，彼諸行轉。如是諸行種子不斷故，諸行得生；諸行生故，得有識轉。如是所餘諸緣起支流轉道理，如其所應，當知亦爾。因名緣起，果名緣生，即此差別。如下決擇分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/56.htm#7363:44708">陵本五十六卷十五頁4543</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一切因緣所生法，需依託眾緣生起現行以後，當因受用已盡，現行法的自性已經滅除。可是在現行生起的同時沒有間斷的在阿賴耶識中熏成種子，種子相續而生，雖然經過很久的時間，因為有種子在，只要眾緣具足，還能令可愛的或不可愛的果報變異成熟，這是依因性而稱為緣起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《緣起經》中說：此有故彼有，此生故彼生。應該知道是指因為有無明種子相續不斷的緣故，眾緣具足彼無明的現行就會生起；此無明的現行生起，彼福行、非福行、不動行的諸行就會生起。福等諸行造作時同時熏成種子，如是諸行種子未斷故，諸行得生；諸行生故，就有隨業識轉生而起。如是所餘諸緣起支，如識緣名色，乃至生緣老死的流轉道理，因有前支的種子而有前支的現行，是此有故彼有，因前支的現行生起引生後支生起，是此生故彼生，應當知道也是如此。在這裡，因是指此有故彼有，名為緣起，果是指此生故彼生，名為緣生，這是其中的差別。這些差別如〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷56，1862頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉四、依數壞數滅義釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科依數壞數滅義釋，依數壞數滅義理來解釋緣起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，數數謝滅，復相續起，故名緣起。此依數壞數滅義釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，有情的果報體一次又一次的死後，又相續生起，例如在人中死了，又到畜生道去受生，因此名為緣起。這是依數壞數滅義解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》數數謝滅等者：此說苦果死生相續應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一次又一次的死後又生，這是說異熟苦果死生相續，應該要知道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉五、依等覺義釋2　戌一、標義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科依等覺義釋，依平等覺悟義解釋緣起，分二科；第一科標義，標出義理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，於過去世覺緣性已，等相續起，故名緣起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，佛陀於過去世時覺悟了緣起緣性的道理，與內心覺悟的道理如實相等相續宣說緣起，因此名為緣起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、引證</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科引證，引佛所說的話為證。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如世尊言：我已覺悟，正起宣說，即由此名展轉傳說，故名緣起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如佛陀說：我已經覺悟了緣起的法，也同我所覺悟的一樣，平等宣說緣起法，就由這個名稱展轉的傳說，稱為緣起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p751"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於過去世覺緣性已等者：緣起聖道經說：曾見老死，見老死集，見老死滅，見於老死趣滅行跡；如是曾見生、有、取、愛、受、觸、六處、名色、識、行，曾見行集，曾見行滅，曾見於行趣滅行跡。我於此法自然通達，現等覺已，乃至廣說是諸苾芻若於此中能修正行，成能證者，便能證得正理法善。此中諸義，準彼應釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《緣起聖道經》說：我曾經看過眾生有種種的老死，也看見集聚老死的原因，看到老死謝滅，也看到老死趣滅的行跡，通達如何修道才能夠滅除老死的苦惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於曾經體驗到五蘊的生命體是由有而來的；有是由取而來；取是由愛而來的；愛是由受來的；受是由觸來的；觸是由六處來的，六處是由名色而來的；名色是由識來；識是由行來的。我也曾經見到有行的集聚，曾經見到行滅，曾經見到於行趣滅行的道跡。我對於緣起法，已無師自悟自然的通達，而且示現平等覺悟緣起實相的道理，乃至詳細說若是諸多比丘能於緣起法正確的修行，成為能證聖道的修行人，便能夠證得於過去世、現在世及未來世都能順於正理、利益眾生的緣起實相的善法。此中種種道理，應當準照《緣起聖道經》所說解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未七、緣起緣性2　申一、辨緣性2　酉一、舉無明望行2　戌一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科緣起緣性，說明緣起的緣性，指十二支互相為緣的性質，分二科；第一科辨緣性，說明緣的體性，又分二科；第一科舉無明望行，說明無明和行的關係，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="7666:7374"></a>問：無明望行為幾種緣？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：無明對望於行有幾種緣？無明是內心的煩惱，行有身語意三行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、答2　亥一、辨二種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科辨二種，辨別二種緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：望諸色行為增上緣，望無色行為三緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：無明對望於身語的色行是增上緣，對望於無色的意行有所緣緣、等無間緣、增上緣三緣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無明是內心的煩惱，對所知事不了解，不知道我空法空的道理，望諸色行，色行就是身行和語行，即身業和語業。「對望諸色行為增上緣」是指無明能夠有力量，幫助推動身業和語業的造作，無明煩惱與思心所相應能夠推有情動身發語，是身業和語業等色行的增上緣。「望無色行為三緣」，無色行就是意行，對望意行有三種緣。由現行無明前一剎那滅，能引發後一剎那無色意行生，因為有無明，前一剎那無明，下一剎那行就生出來了，這是等無間緣；行生出來的時候，又緣著無明而造業，例如計執最勝等不如理思惟，這時所緣邪見與無明相應，因此也是無色意行的所緣緣；由無明的增上力令相應思顛倒緣境而造作諸業，因此無明望行也是增上緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋三緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋三緣，解釋三種緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂等無間緣、所緣緣、增上緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三緣是指等無間緣、所緣緣、增上緣三緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》望諸色行為增上緣等者：此中色行，謂身語業；又無色行，謂即意業應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行有三種，其中的色行就是身業和語業，無色行就是意業應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、例餘支相望2　戌一、標例</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘支相望，例出其餘諸支相望，分二科；第一科標例，標示例舉出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是餘支為緣多少，應如此知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是其餘諸支互相為緣有多少？應該依此推理可知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、別辨2　亥一、約有色支辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別辨，各別的說明，分二科；第一科約有色支辨，以有色支說明緣性。十二緣起中有色支是指色法，無色支是指心心所法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p752"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有色支望有色支，為一增上緣；望無色支為二緣，謂所緣緣及增上緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有色支對望於有色支，是增上緣，例如生支位中現行色望老死支中現行色蘊唯有一增上緣，老死支中色蘊既是色法不能緣境，不須以前生支位中色蘊為所緣境，因此無所緣緣，又色法不從等無間緣生即無等無間緣；對望於無色支，是所緣緣以及增上緣，例如生支位中現行色法能為後老死支中現行心心所法所緣，因此說有色支望無色支為所緣緣，生支中現行色法如眼根，能為後老死支中現行心心所法，如眼識所依，因此說有色支望無色支為增上緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、約無色支辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約無色支辨，約無色支說明緣性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若無色支望有色支，唯為一緣；望無色支為三緣，謂等無間緣、所緣緣、增上緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是無色支對望有色支，只有一個增上緣，例如色法不從無間緣生故，或無明望身語業也是無色望有色，如前所說無明對望於身語的色行是增上緣；無色支對望於無色支，有三種緣，包括等無間緣、所緣緣、及增上緣，如前所說無明對望於無色的意行有所緣緣、等無間緣、增上緣三緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如是餘支為緣多少等者：謂後後支諸緣生法，漸次相稱因果體性相續而生，是此緣性。所說緣義如前。無明望行，由色無色有差別故，說與為緣或多或少；如是後後諸支，前望於後，或為多緣、或為少緣，隨應當知。總略而言：若前為有色支，與後有色支或無色支為緣；及前為無色支，與後有色支或無色支為緣；隨應差別，如文可悉。然非一一支中，前望於後，定有如是差別。或為有色、或為無色，或全、或分，隨其所應盡當知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　相對於前支，所說的後後支諸緣生法，漸次由因與果相稱的體性相續而生，就是這裡所說的緣性。所說緣義如前所說除因緣外，有三種緣中的或多或少。無明望於行，由色法與無色法有差別的緣故，說與色法為緣或是與非色法為緣，會有或多的所緣緣、增上緣、等無間緣三緣或少的增上緣一緣；由這樣後後諸支，前支望於後支，於非色法為多種緣、有色法為少緣，隨所相應的應當知道。整相及要略而言：如果前為有色支，與後有色支或無色支為緣；以及前為無色支，與後有色支或無色支為緣；隨有色與無色所對應的差別，如文所說可以知道。但並不是一一支中，前望於後，一定是這樣的差別。因為諸支有的或為有色、有的或為無色，或全部、或一部分，隨其所相應應該都推理可知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、釋妨難2　酉一、不說因緣難2　戌一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋妨難，解釋難問，分二科；第一科不說因緣難，解釋十二緣起不說因緣的難問，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何故諸支相望無因緣耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為什麼前支與後支相望，例如無明緣行乃至生緣老死，沒有因緣？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p753"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：因緣者，自體種子緣所顯故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：所謂因緣，是指諸法自體種子緣而言。諸法是自體的種子所顯發的。不是前一支的種子直接生起後一支的，也就是無明必須有無明的種子才能夠產生無明的現行，行也是有行的種子才能夠產生行的現行。就因緣來說，行不是由無明而來的，無明對於行中的色行，只能說是增上緣，無明對於行中的無色行，可以有三種緣，就是等無間、所緣緣和增上緣，都沒有說到因緣，因為因緣是指自體的種子緣，種子對現行來說是因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、說依因果難2　戌一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科說依因果難，說依因果的難問，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若諸支相望無因緣者，何故說言：依因果體性建立緣起耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：若十二支中，無明緣行乃至生緣老死，前後支相對望沒有因緣，也沒有提到種子生現行這件事，為什麼還說是依因果的體性來建立緣起呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、答2　亥一、總明攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科總明攝，總體說明增上緣所攝諸因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依增上緣所攝引發因、牽引因、生起因故，說名為因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：這是依增上緣所含攝的引發因、牽引因、生起因，說名為因。十二緣起是依增上緣所攝的引發因來說。以此為因，能產生另外一法，稱為增上緣；由此法能夠隨順生起另一法，就說此法是能夠引發另一法的引發因。這裡引發因是總說的，包括牽引因及生起因，因為牽引因能生起下一生的果報體，生起因能夠滋潤生下一生的果報體，使種子現行。這些都能隨順於生起果報體，都可以稱為引發因。引發因的範圍很廣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》依增上緣所攝引發因等者：緣起初勝法門經說：唯依一增上緣，說無明緣行，次第乃至生緣老死。此增上緣復有二種，一、遠，二、近。當知遠增上緣，即此所說牽引因；近增上緣，即此所說生起因；前能引後，展轉增勝，即此所說引發因。是故經說唯依一增上緣。此中三因，如前有尋有伺地釋。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/05.htm#7397:3529">陵本五卷十頁358</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《緣起初勝法門經》說：十二緣起只有依止一種增上緣，說無明緣行，次第乃至生緣老死。增上緣又有二種：一、遠的增上緣，是指牽引因，二、近的增上緣，是指生起因；無明緣行，行緣識，是能引的，所引的是識乃至受五法種子。近的增上緣，是受緣愛，愛緣取，取緣有，愛、取、有，是能生的；所生的是生、老、死。前一支能夠引發後一支，展轉的增勝增強，就是這裡所說的引發因。因此經中說只依一種增上緣。此中的引發因、牽引因、生起因三因，如前〈有尋有伺地〉卷5，143頁中有詳細的解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、別配屬3　天一、引因攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別配屬，十二支各別配合三因所攝，分三科；第一科引因攝，說明引因所攝支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾支是引因所攝？答：從無明乃至受。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：幾支是十二支中的引因所攝？答：從無明開始，行、識、名色、六入、觸直到受，這六支是引因所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p754"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、生因攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科生因攝，說明生因所攝支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾支是生因所攝？答：從愛乃至有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：幾支是生因所攝？答：從愛開始，加上取及有，是能生支所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、二果攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科二果攝，說明二種果所攝支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾支是生、引二因果所攝耶？答：於現法後法中，識等乃至受，於生、老死位所攝諸支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：幾支是生因與引因這二種因所攝的果呢？答：於現法中，能引的因是無明與行，所引的果是識、名色、六入、觸、受五法種子；於後法中，愛、取、有是能生因；生、老、死是所生的果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於現法後法中識等乃至受等者：此中識言，謂隨業識，由此故說於現法中。此識為後有名色、六處、觸、受種子之所隨逐，由此故說於後法中。如是一切，當知皆是引因果攝。生、老死位識乃至受，名彼所攝諸支，當知此是生因果攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處所說的識字，是指隨業識，這識裡面有業的種子隨逐，稱隨業識，因此說在現法中。這識中有名色、六入、觸、受種子之所隨逐，強調的是種子的形態，由於這些種子在將來的生命體才會得到現行，所以說是於後法中。如是這一切，以現法說，識、名色、六入、觸、受應當知道都是引因的果所攝。以後法說，生、老死位，是愛、取、有結合識、名色、六入、觸、受的生因之果所攝，因此合說現法、後法中，識等乃至受，於生、老死位所攝諸支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未八、緣起分別緣9　申一、十二支次第分別2　酉一、辨為緣11　戌一、無明緣行2　亥一、望與無明為緣2　天一、約不如理作意辨2　地一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科緣起分別緣，十二緣起的次第等分別緣，分九科；第一科十二支次第分別，說明十二支次第的分別，又分二科；第一科辨為緣，說明十二緣起前支為後支緣，又分十一科；第一科無明緣行，無明為緣生行，又分二科；第一科望與無明為緣，說明與無明為緣，又分二科；第一科約不如理作意辨，說明以不如理作意為無明緣，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="48758:7407"></a>問：若說無明以不如理作意為因，何因緣故於緣起教中不先說耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如果說無明以不如理作意為因，為什麼十二緣起不先說不如理作意緣無明，無明緣行？人為什麼會有無明？就是因為有不如理作意，不合事情的真理，內心這樣子想，就會有無明。為什麼不先這樣說？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、答4　玄一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分四科；第一科標，標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p755"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：彼唯是不斷因故，非雜染因故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：不如理作意，是五遍行心所中的作意心所被無明所染汙，唯是無明不能斷除的原因，並不是能夠雜染無明的原因。不如理作意自性不是雜染，所以不攝在緣起支中。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》彼唯是不斷因故等者：謂不如理作意唯能障彼無明對治，是故名彼是不斷因。然由不能染汙無明，是故名彼非雜染因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不如理作意只是能障礙無明的對治，因此名不如理作意是無明不能斷除的原因。由於不如理作意不能染污無明，因此說不如理作意不是雜染因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼這樣說？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄三、釋2　黃一、由非染汙</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科由非染污，由於不如理作意自性非染污。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">非不愚者起此作意。依雜染因說緣起教，無明自性是染汙，不如理作意自性非染汙，故彼不能染汙無明，然由無明力所染汙。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不是不愚癡的人會生起這種作意，換句話說只有沒有智慧、愚癡的人才會生起不如理作意。佛依雜染因來說緣起的教理，無明的體性是染污的，不如理作意的體性不是染污的，它不能夠染汙無明，然而卻是由無明力所染汙的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》非不愚者起此作意者：謂不如理作意亦以無明為因而生。若諸聖者無明斷已，此不如理作意亦無。由此釋前彼唯是不斷因，謂唯無明未斷時，說以不如理作意為因故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不如理作意也是因為以無明為因而生。若是諸多成就聖道的聖人將無明斷除以後，這不如理作意也不會再生起了。由這裡解釋前面不如理作意只是無明不能斷除的一項原因，是說無明沒有斷除時，仍會以不如理作意為因的緣故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、由非業因</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由非業因，說明不如理作意不是真正的業因，真正的業因是無明煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又生雜染業煩惱力之所熏發，業之初因謂初緣起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有生的雜染，主要是由於業及煩惱的力量之所熏習與引發造成，業會生起的初因是指最初緣起的無明煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p756"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄四、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科結，結說不說不如理作意。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故不說不如理作意。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所以在緣起支中不先說不如理作意。不如理作意是與煩惱相應的作意，明確的指出來煩惱及業主要是由無明引發，而不是不如理作意。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又生雜染至謂初緣起者：此說無明能為煩惱、業、生三種雜染根本因緣。如緣起初勝法門經說：無明普於一切煩惱雜染、諸業雜染、諸生雜染能作因緣根本依處。是故無明由殊勝故，建立初支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡是說煩惱雜染、業雜染、生雜染三種雜染最根本的因緣就是無明。如《緣起初勝法門經》所說：無明普遍存在於一切煩惱雜染、諸業雜染、生雜染中，無明能作為三種雜染因緣的根本依止處。因此是由於無明煩惱力量殊勝的原因，而以無明建立十二有支中的初支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、約自體辨2　地一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約自體辨，約自體說明，分二科；第一科問，提問。前面是約不如理作意來說明，為什麼要建立無明為初支，現在是約自體來說明這件事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何故不說自體為自體緣耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為什麼不說無明自體為無明自體的緣呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：由彼自體若不得餘緣，於自體雜染不能增長，亦不損減，是故不說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：由於無明自體不能為自體的緣，如果沒有得到其他的增上緣，對於無明自體的雜染不能增長，也不會損減，因此不說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》何故不說自體為自體緣等者：此中問答，且約無明為論，當知非不遍通一切，無明為初，是故舉說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這其中的問答，是約無明為論，應當知道自體不能為自體緣並非不是遍通於一切十二支，十二支中諸支都是自體不能為自體緣，然而無明是十二支中的初支，而且無明煩惱的力量殊勝，因此舉無明為例說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、望與行為緣3　天一、約二愚辨2　地一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科望與行為緣，無明能夠給行做緣，分三科；第一科約二愚辨，約二種愚癡說明，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何因緣故，福行、不動行由正揀擇功力而起，仍說用無明為緣耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：什麼因緣有些人造作種種的善事等福行，及修禪定等不動行，這些都是因爲具有智慧能正確揀擇的功德力而生起的，為什麼仍然說也是以無明為緣呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p757"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>
