<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：由不了達世俗苦因為緣，起非福行；由不了達勝義苦因為緣，生福及不動行；是故亦說彼以無明為緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：主要是由於不了解及沒有通達世俗的苦因為緣，而生起非福行的不善業；由於不了解及沒有通達勝義苦的因為緣，而生起福行及不動行；因此造作福行及不動行也說是以無明為緣。有一些人知道善因善果、惡因惡果，想要積聚人天的福報，或是想離欲修禪定，即使修到三界之頂，這些都還是人天善法，由於不能通達無常變異、遷流不息的行苦，及不能通達無我的真義，仍有我、我所等我執的無明戲論種子隨逐，不能了解勝義苦，終究還是會在三界流轉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由不了達世俗苦因為緣等者：苦苦、壞苦，名世俗苦；行麤重苦，名勝義苦。世俗苦因，即苦樂受；勝義苦因，即不苦不樂受。如諸愚夫於樂受中多生染著，及於苦受多生瞋心，由是因緣起非福行。又於不苦不樂受中心生顛倒。見勝功德，或見出離，故造福行及不動行。造斯行時，雖依教法或依誨法，發起思擇及修習心；然不如理作意思惟，於見功德或見出離，癡所覆藏；是故亦說彼以無明為緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　苦的痛苦、變壞的痛苦，名為世俗苦；遷流不息麤重的行苦，名為勝義苦。世俗的苦因，是來自於苦受及樂受變壞之苦；勝義的苦因，是來自於難以覺察的不苦不樂受。例如諸多愚癡無聞的凡夫對於所生起的樂受中多分會生起貪愛染著，及對於生起的苦受多分會生起瞋心，由此因緣而造作非福業的惡行。又對於難以覺察的不苦不樂受及遷流不息的行苦，如不苦不樂受相應的第四禪及四空定等，心中生起顛倒，並不認為是苦。觀見造善的殊勝功德，或是觀見禪定能出離欲界的苦惱，因此造作福行的善業及修禪定等不動行。造作這類福行及不動行時，雖然是依止聖教所教導的修習禪觀的方法或依止聖教所訓斥教誨的諸惡莫作、眾善奉行的福分等善法，來發起思惟決擇及修習的心；然而由於無明所引的不如理作意思惟，雖然能觀見殊勝功德或能觀見必須出離欲界苦惱，仍是被愚癡所覆蓋隱藏，不能真正出離三界，斷除無明；所以也說造作福行及不動行以無明為緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、約三業辨2　地一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約三業辨，約福業、非福業、和不動業三種業來説明，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：如經中說：諸業以貪瞋癡為緣。何故此中唯說癡為緣耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如經中說：所有的業都是以貪瞋癡為緣，為什麽這裡只有說癡，就是無明為緣呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：此中通說福、非福、不動業緣，貪瞋癡緣唯生非福業故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：此處通說福、非福、不動業為無明的緣所引發，範圍比較廣，包括修善事的福業，造惡的非福業，及修禪定的不動業，都是以無明為緣；以貪瞋癡為緣只會造惡業，所以不說貪瞋癡為緣，而說無明為緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p758"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此中通說福非福不動業緣者：無明為緣遍一切業，已如前說。今顯福、不動業，彼以無貪、無瞋為其因緣，非貪、瞋起。貪、瞋不遍，是故不說；唯無明遍，故偏說之。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因爲以無明為緣，能遍一切福、非福及不動業業，已如前文所說。這裡顯示修福業及不動業，必須要以無貪無瞋為因緣，沒有貪瞋的心才會去修福業和不動業。貪、瞋不能遍於十二支，所以不說貪、瞋。只有無明是遍一切煩惱、遍一切行、遍十二支，因此說無明緣行。不說貪瞋癡緣行，因爲貪瞋癡只會推動非福行，不會推動福行及不動行，故說以無明為緣，這樣的說法才比較周延。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、約遍行辨2　地一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科約遍行辨，約遍行心所來說明，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：身業、語業思所發起，是則行亦緣行；何故但說無明緣行？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：身業、語業是由思心所所發動的，如此行也是緣行，為什麽只說無明緣行？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依發起一切行緣而說故，及依生善、染汙思緣而說故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：說無明緣行是依止著無明能發起身語意一切行為緣而說的，而思只能發動身行及語行，這是第一個理由。第二個理由是無明可以推動善思，也可以推動染汙的不善思，它的範圍很廣，因此說無明緣行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》依發起一切行緣而說故等者：身語意行，名一切行，無明遍發，是故說之。思發身語，唯二非遍，是故不說。又無明為緣，能生善、染汙思，業用殊勝，是故說之。思發身語，或時無記，業用非勝，是故不說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　身行、語行、意行稱為一切行，無明普遍能夠發動這三種行，因此說無明緣行。思只能發動身語二種而不能遍於三種行，因此不說。又無明為緣，能夠生出善思、染汙思，於非福業的時候有染汙思，於福業及不動業時有善思，它的作用特別殊勝，因此說無明緣行。思心所發動的身業、語業，有時是無記，作用功能不如無明殊勝，因此不說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、行緣識2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科行緣識，說明行緣識，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：識亦以名色為緣，何故此中但說行為緣耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：識也是要以名色為緣，識緣名色，名色緣識，不是互相為緣嗎，為什麽這裡只有說行為緣呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p759"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：行為識雜染緣，能引、能生後有果故。非如名色，但為所依、所緣，生起緣故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：因為福行、非福行及動行，能夠成為識的雜染緣，行的同時熏習識乃至受五法的種子，能夠引發及生出將來的異熟識。不像名色支，只是現行識所依、所緣的境界，是識生起的緣，但是不能引生後有的異熟識。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》行為識雜染緣等者：謂異熟識為一切諸業雜染之所熏習，由此方便，攝受後有新生種子，於當生中所起後有所攝名色、六處、觸、受次第而生，此名色等即後有果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　異熟識，果報體的識，是由於一切善、不善諸業雜染的熏習成就的，由於業雜染的熏習，能夠攝持後有的新生種子，這些新生的種子，於將來的生支中生起識的現行後，後有果報識中所攝的名色、六處、觸、受，四法就會次第而生，這些名色等支就是下一生的果報。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、識緣名色2　亥一、約大種及觸辨2　天一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科識緣名色，說明識緣名色，分二科；第一科約大種及觸辨，以地水火風四大種及觸來説明識緣名色的關係，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：名色亦由大種所造及由觸生，何故但說識為緣耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：名色也是由地水火風大種所造及由觸對境界而生，為什麼只說識為緣呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：識能為彼新生因故。彼既生已，或正生時，大種及觸唯能與彼為建立因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：阿賴耶識能作為名色新生的因。名色既然生起，或在正生時，地水火風大種及觸只能成為名色的建立因，不是使令新名色生起來的主要原因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》識能為彼新生因故等者：此中生因，謂為前導。又建立因，謂同安危。如前意地說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/03.htm#7455:1686">陵本三卷一頁183</a>）初受生時，識最為先，依此建立新異熟識。由是名色次第而生，是故說識與彼名色為新生因。識為前導，名色方生，故名色生已，或正生時，大種身根和合而有，安危共同，是故說言大種及觸唯與名色為建立因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這其中的生因，是指識為前導，有了識才能夠有名色。又建立因，是指由大種損益。造色同安危故。如前面《意地》卷3，80頁所說。剛去投生時，最先阿賴耶識入母胎，依止阿賴耶識建立一個新的異熟識。識入母胎同時與父精母卵和合在一起，變成名色的羯羅藍位，由此名色、六處等次第生起，因此說識與名色為新生因。由阿賴耶識為前導，名色才能生起，名色生起已後，或正在生時，諸根大種與身根及根所依大種和合而有；由大種損益，身根也受損益，因此說地水火風大種及觸只是名色的建立因。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在〈意地〉卷3，79～81頁說：諸大種望所造色，有生因、持因、依因、建立因、養因五種作用，其中由大種損益，彼同安危故，說明建立因，此處披尋記說的建立因是約由大種損益，彼造色同安危義而解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p760"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、約六界入胎辨2　天一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約六界入胎辨，以地水火風空識六界為緣入胎說明，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：如經中說：六界為緣得入母胎。何故此中唯說識界？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如經中所說：地、水、火、風、空、識六界為緣得入母胎，為什麼此處只說六界中的識界入母胎？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、答3　地一、由定俱</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科由定俱，由有識其餘地水火風空五界一定同時具備。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：若有識界，決定於母胎中精血、大種、腹穴無闕故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：因為有識界，在母胎中決定有父精母卵的精血、諸根大種的地水火風，腹穴的空，因此地水火風與空就沒有缺少了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、由最勝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由最勝，由於識界的力量是最強的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又識界勝故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由於識界的力量是最殊勝的。因為如果有識，一定會有地水火風空這五法，有其它五法不一定會有識，所以由定俱來説是識入母胎，故說識緣名色，而不說六界緣名色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若有識界等者：界有六種，謂地、水、火、風、空、識。聲聞地說：云何識界？謂眼、耳、鼻、舌、身、意識，又心、意、識三種差別，是名識界。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/27.htm#7463:22383">陵本二十七卷三頁2253</a>）於母胎中，精血、大種，意顯地水火風四界；又彼腹穴，意顯空界。入母胎時，若有識界，餘定無闕，是故此中唯說識界。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　界有六種，包括地、水、火、風、空、識。〈聲聞地〉說：什麼稱為識界？是指眼、耳、鼻、舌、身、意識，這六識稱為識界；又心、意、識的六、七、八識三種差別，也名為識界。如〈聲聞地〉卷27，915頁中所說。在母胎中，所說的精血、大種，意思可以顯示有地水火風四種界；又身中的腹穴空隙，意思顯示有空界。肚子裏面的空隙稱為空界。入母胎時，如果有識界，其餘地水火風空界一定不會缺少，因此在緣起中只說識界，只說識緣名色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地三、由遍行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科由遍行，說明識遍行於一切界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p761"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又依一切生、一切有生時而說故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又識是依一切生、一切有生時而說故。一切生就是胎卵溼化四生，一切有，欲有、色有、無色有，或者是人、天、地獄、餓鬼、畜牲五趣也可以稱為有，有這二種解釋。在一切胎卵溼化的生命體裏面，或者是五趣的眾生，或者是三界的眾生來說，於生的時候一定會有識的，所以說識緣名色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又依一切生一切有生時而說故者：胎、卵、濕、化四生，名一切生。那落迦等五有，名一切有。識遍一切，是故說之。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　胎、卵、濕、化四種生，名為一切生。那落迦、旁生、餓鬼、人、天五有，名為一切有。識是普遍存在於四種生、五趣有，所以說識緣名色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌四、名色緣六處2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科名色緣六處，說明有名色就會有六處，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：六處亦以飲食為緣，何故此中但說名色為緣耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：六處也是以飲食為緣，為什麽緣起中只說名色為六處的緣呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：此中說名色是彼生因故。彼既生已，亦以飲食為任持因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：緣起中是說名色是六處的生因。六處生出來以後，也是以飲食為它保任執持的因，使令它能夠繼續存在及增長。因此說名色緣六處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》亦以飲食為任持因者：由飲食故，六處得住，是故說彼為任持因，任持六處令不壞故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為有飲食，使名色及六處得以相續安住，因此說飲食為任持因，能任持名色及六處令不爛壞。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌五、六處緣觸2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科六處緣觸，說明六處緣觸，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：觸以三和為緣，何故此中但說六處為緣？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：觸以根、塵、識三和合為緣，為什麽緣起中只有說六處為緣？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答2　天一、由定俱</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科由定俱，只要有根其餘二法一定會有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：若有六處，定有餘二無闕故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：如果具備有六處，一定有其餘六塵與六識，二種不會缺少。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p762"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、由最勝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由最勝，說明六處在根、塵、識中是最勝的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又六處勝故，由六處攝二種故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又六處在六根、六塵、六識中是最勝的，由六處可以含攝六塵、六識二種，因為要依根才能夠緣境發識，根、塵、識三法和合能生觸，所以最主要還是要有六根，沒有六根就不能觸對境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若有六處等者：六處謂根，餘二謂境與識。識依根生，境由根顯，根攝二種，是故最勝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六處是指根，其餘二法是指境、與識。識必須依根才能生識，境界也是由根才能顯現，根能攝持境與識二種，所以說是最勝。因此說六處緣觸。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌六、觸緣受2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科觸緣受，說明觸緣受，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若自所逼迫，若他所逼迫，若時候變異，若先業所引，皆得生受；何故此中但顯觸為彼緣？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如果是自己逼迫自己，或是別人逼迫自己，或是季節、天候有變異，或是過去的業力所引發的，都會生起感受；為什麽緣起中只顯示觸為受的緣？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：觸是彼近因故，由觸所引故；餘緣所生受亦從觸生故，必不離觸，是故偏說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：因為觸是生起受最接近的原因，由觸對境界才能引發身心的感受；其他的因緣所生的受也是從觸所生的，必然不會離開觸，因此偏說觸緣受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》觸是彼近因等者：觸為受因，由觸為先，受方生故。如順樂受觸為緣，生樂受；順苦受觸為緣，生苦受；順不苦不樂受觸為緣，生不苦不樂受。觸望餘緣生受近故，是故說觸是彼近因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　觸是受的因，一定有觸在先，受才會生起。例如隨順樂受的觸為緣，會生起樂受；隨順苦受的觸為緣，會生起苦受；隨順不苦不樂受的觸為緣，會生起不苦不樂受。觸相對於其他會生起受的緣是最近的因，因此說觸是受的近因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p763"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌七、受緣愛2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科受緣愛，說明受緣愛，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：經中亦說無明為緣生愛，順愛境界亦得為緣，何故此中但說受為緣耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：經中也說由無明煩惱為緣會生起愛，隨順可愛的境界，也會由可愛境界為緣生起愛煩惱，為何緣起中只說以受為緣的受緣愛呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》順愛境界亦得為緣者：若可意事、不可意事為所緣時，是名順愛境界。由可意事順和合愛，不可意事順乖離愛，由是故說順愛境界亦得為緣生愛。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果是以可令人滿意的事、或是不可令人滿意的事為所緣時，稱為順愛境界。由可令人滿意的事會隨順生起和合愛，由不可令人滿意的事會隨順生起乖離愛，由此說順愛境界也可為緣生起和合愛或乖離愛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答2　天一、顯正</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科顯正，顯示正確的說法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：以受力故，於相似境，或求和合，或求乖離。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：這是以受的力量，於相似的境界，於可愛境希求和合，於不可愛境希求乖離。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》以受力故至或求乖離者：謂由受力領納現前苦樂異熟或境界時，若為樂受之所纏逼，便於彼相似境起和合愛，希求未來還受如是受故；若為苦受之所纏逼，便於彼相似境起乖離愛，希求未來不受如是受故。由是道理，經中唯說受為愛緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是說由受的力量領納現前的苦或樂異熟或是境界時，如果被樂受之所纏繞逼迫，就會於樂受相似的境界生起和合愛，希望未來再受這類有可愛的受；如果被苦受之所纏繞逼迫，就會於苦受相似的境生起乖離愛，希望未來不再受這類不可愛的受。由這種道理，經中只說受為愛緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、簡非</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡非，簡除不是的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由愚癡力，但於諸受起盡等相不如實知，由此不能制御其心。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於有無明煩惱、愚癡的力量，使令有情對於苦受、樂受、和不苦不樂受的生起與消滅的種種相狀，不能如實了知，因此當有感受生出來時，苦的時候多分生起瞋心，快樂的時候多分生起貪心，不苦不樂受的時候多分生起癡心，不能控制自己的心。只有聖人才知道諸受皆苦，能修行斷受，不隨受轉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p764"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由愚癡力至不能制御其心者。於諸受中有八相別：謂受有幾種，誰是受集，誰是受滅，誰是受集趣行，誰是受滅趣行，誰是受愛味，誰是受過患，誰是受出離，是名諸受起盡等相。由愚癡力，於此不能如理觀察，是故不能如實了知；不了知故，於妙五欲染汙希求，是故不能制御其心。由是道理，經中亦說無明為緣生愛，然非近因，此不說之。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於諸受中有八種差別相貌：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、受有幾種，這是觀察受的自相，也是觀察苦諦，五識相應受有苦受、樂受、不苦不樂受三種，意識相應受有苦受、憂受、喜受、樂受、不苦不樂受五種；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、誰是受集，什麽原因會有受？這是觀察現法觸為現法受的原因，也是觀察集諦的同時因果，由觸集故受集；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、誰是受滅，怎麽樣可以滅除諸受？這是觀現法受滅，也是觀察滅諦，由觸滅故受滅；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、誰是受集趣行，是誰使令受積聚，這是觀後法受生起的原因，也是觀察集諦的異時因果，由無明相應觸生愛見煩惱造善惡業，是後法受（未來受）生起的原因；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、誰是受滅趣行，如何使令受趣向寂滅？這是觀察斷除後法受的原因，也是觀察道諦，修習戒定慧斷除無明相應觸，令愛見煩惱不生，不造善惡業，是斷除後法受（未來受）的原因；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、誰是受愛味，這是觀察觸及受二法生起的原因，於受愛味能生長現法受的因觸及後法受的因業及無明相應觸，這是重觀苦諦和集諦；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、誰是受過患，受的過患是什麼？這是觀察受有現法、後法及現法後法過患，能生疾病苦、惡趣苦及老死苦，也是觀道諦，觀受過患之時能滅除於現法及後法二種受的因；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、誰是受出離，怎麽樣可以出離受的過患呢？這是觀察出離諸受獲得清淨，如三摩呬多地說到出諸受事，初靜慮出離憂根，第二靜慮出離苦根，第三靜慮出離喜根，第四靜慮出離樂根，於無相界出離捨根，唯有斷除分別起及俱生起的我執無明等煩惱，才能究竟出離諸受。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於受到無明愚癡力的影響，於此諸受不能如諸法實相的真理來觀察，因此不能如實了知種種受的情況；由於不了知的緣故，對於世間微妙的五欲就會有染汙希求，因此不能克制駕御自己的心。由於這種道理，經中也說以無明為緣可以產生愛，可是它不是最近的原因，因此這裡不說，只說受緣愛，不說無明緣愛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌八、愛緣取2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科愛緣取，說明愛緣取，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：由隨眠未斷，順彼諸法取皆得生，何故此中但說愛為取緣？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：由於煩惱種子沒有斷，隨順煩惱種子生起煩惱現行時，各種取就會產生，爲什麽這裡只說愛為取緣？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由隨眠未斷順彼諸法取皆得生者：此中隨眠，謂欲貪隨眠及見隨眠。由欲貪隨眠未斷故，欲取得生；由見隨眠未斷故，見取、戒禁取、我語取得生。為得諸欲及為受用，乃至為欲隨說諸士夫相諸所為取，是名順彼諸法，由能隨順生欲貪故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡所說的隨眠（煩惱種子），主要說的是欲貪以及見煩惱的種子。因爲欲貪的煩惱種子沒有斷除，緣欲貪的現行就會有欲取生起；由於見煩惱的種子沒有斷除，緣各種見的現行就會有見取、戒禁取和我語取生起。爲了得到諸欲、受用諸欲，就會生起欲取；爲了詰責他所立論，或者是免脫他所徵難，就會生起見取；爲了修定，往趣世間離欲乃至非想非非想處三摩缽底，就會生起戒禁取；爲了隨說分別所計所執著的造業的人、受果的人，或者是說流轉的人、或者是還滅的人，就會生起我語的取著，如是諸所為取名為順彼諸法，這是由於諸所為取能隨順所希求的境界而生起欲貪的緣故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：由希望生故，於追求時，能發隨眠，及能引彼隨順法故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：由於内心有愛生而生欲求，於追求時，就能夠發動欲取乃至我語取的煩惱種子產生現行，以及能夠引生出隨順四取現行的諸所為取。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p765"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由希望生故等者：謂由愛相希望生故，於三界行染汙希求時，隨其所應，能發欲貪及見隨眠生現行纏，及能引導諸所為取隨順法故，由是故說愛為取緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由有愛煩惱現行，種種希求就產生了，於三界諸行有染汙希求時，隨所相應的境界，能引發欲貪及見煩惱種子生現行，及能引導四種所為取隨順法，因此說愛為取的緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌九、取緣有2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科取緣有，說明取緣有，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：前已說無明為緣發起業有，何故今者說取緣有？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：前面已說無明緣行，無明為緣可以發起業有，為什麼現在要說取緣有？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：由取力故，即令彼業於彼彼生處能引識、名色等果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：由於取的力量，能引發後有業，在五趣不同的受生處所，成就所引的識、名色六入觸受這五法的果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌十、有緣生2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科有緣生，說明有緣生，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：生亦以精血等為緣，何故此中唯說有緣生耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：受生時也以父精母血，及三處現前等為緣，為什麼緣起中只說有緣生呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答2　天一、由定俱</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科由定俱，由有定有其他的緣一定同時存在。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：由有有故，定有餘緣無闕。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：只要有「有」的生起，一定有其他的因緣來配合。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、由最勝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由最勝，說明由「有」的緣相較於其他的緣為最勝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有勝故，唯說彼為緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由於「有」的力量最強勝，「有」是引發「生」現行的緣，因此說以有為緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌十一、生緣老死2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十一科生緣老死，說明生緣老死，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p766"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：亦由遠行、不避不平等、他所逼迫為緣，老死可得，何故此中但說生緣老死耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：於遠路而行，不迴避種種不平等能危害身心的因緣、或被他人逼迫惱害的因緣，也都有可能會有老死，為什麼於緣起中只說由生緣老死呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：雖由彼諸緣，必以生為根本故。縱闕彼緣，但生為緣，定有老死故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：雖然由種種諸緣也會老死，但必定是以生為根本。縱然缺少其他的緣，但只要有生為緣，一定有老死。這是不會改變的原則，其他的都可以避免，可是生緣老死是不可避免的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》亦由遠行等者：此說諸行敗壞因緣。諸行生已，由彼不能相似相續而住，故有老死可得。不避不平等，如前意地已辨其相。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/01.htm#7519:541">陵本一卷十三頁66</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡是說五蘊諸行敗壞的因緣。五蘊生出來以後，由於剎那生滅無常，不能前後相似、相續而住，所以有老死可得。所說的不避不平等，如前〈意地〉卷1，32頁已有說明及分辨其相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、明彼攝3　戌一、約煩惱等道辨2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明彼攝，說明十二支為煩惱等所攝，分三科；第一科約煩惱等道辨，說明煩惱道、業道、及苦道，惑業苦三道所攝支，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：此十二支，幾是煩惱道？幾是業道？幾是苦道？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：這十二支中，哪些是煩惱道？哪些是業道？哪些是苦道？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：三是煩惱道，二是業道，餘是苦道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：無明、愛、取三支是煩惱道，行、有二支是業道，其餘識、名色、六處、觸、受、生、及老死等七支是苦道。有一偈頌說：無明愛取三煩惱，行有二支屬業道，從識至受並老死，世世常行業苦道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》三是煩惱道等者：三謂無明、愛、取，煩惱雜染攝故；二謂行、有，業雜染攝故；餘支，生雜染攝；依此建立三道差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三是指無明、愛、取，這三支屬於煩惱雜染所攝；二是指行、有，這二支屬於業雜染所攝；其餘從識至受乃至老死，這七支屬於生雜染所攝；依此建立煩惱雜染道、業雜染道、生雜染道三道差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《俱舍論頌疏論本》卷10〈分別根品二之一〉說了一個煩惱、業、苦三道的偈頌：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　「此中說煩惱，如種復如龍，如草根樹莖，及如糠裹米；業如有糠米，如草藥如華；諸異熟果事，如成熟飲食」前四句以龍、草根、樹莖、及糠裹米譬喻顯示煩惱的相狀，次二句以有糠米、草藥、及華，譬喻顯示業因的相狀，後二句以成熟飲食譬喻顯示異熟果的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱如種，是說如從種子而有芽莖等生，譬喻從煩惱能生煩惱及業果；煩惱如龍，是說如龍鎮住池水使水恒流不令枯竭，譬喻煩惱鎮守住業，感果無窮；煩惱如草根，是說如草根未拔；苗剪剪還生，譬喻未拔煩惱根，雖然諸法任運趣向寂滅但滅了又會生起；煩惱如樹莖，是說如樹莖頻生枝葉華果，譬喻從諸煩惱，數起惑業苦；煩惱如糠裹米，是說如糠裹米能生芽等，譬喻煩惱裹住業能招感餘生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　業如有糠米，是說如米有糠能生芽等，譬喻業有煩惱雜染在其中，能招感異熟；業如草藥，是說如諸草藥果熟為後邊，譬喻業果成熟已後，有受盡相，更不招感餘生異熟；業如華，是說如華於果為生近因，譬喻業為近因，能生異熟果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　果如成熟飲食，是說如已煮熟的飲食但應受用，不可能又復轉變成其餘的飲食，譬喻異熟果報既成熟已後，不能更招感餘生異熟。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、約因果等辨2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約因果等辨，約因果等所攝支辨明十二有支，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p767"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾唯是因？幾唯是果？幾通因果？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：十二支中哪幾支只是因？哪幾支是果？哪幾支通因果？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答2　天一、第一義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科第一義，先以第一種道理說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：初一唯因，後一唯果，餘通因果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：第一支是無明，無明只是因，由於有無明才有行，最後一支老死只是果，因為有生必定有老死，其他中間十支通於因及果。例如行是無明的果，但是行是識的因；識是行的果，識又是名色的因，依此類推，可知中間十支通於因果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》初一唯因等者：初一謂無明，能染汙餘，不為餘染，故說唯因。後一謂老死，為餘染汙，不能染餘，故說唯果。餘一切支，能染汙餘，亦為餘染，故通因果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　初一支是無明，能染汙其餘十一支，無明不會被其餘支所染污，所以說唯是因。最後一支是老死，是被其餘支所染汙，而不能染污其餘十一支，所以說唯是果。其餘中間十支能染污別支也能夠被別支所染，所以中間十支通於因果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、第二義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二義，以第二種道理說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又即於此問，更作餘答：三唯是因，二唯是果，當知所餘亦因亦果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又對這問題還有其他的答案：無明、愛、取，三支唯是因；生及老死，二支唯是果；應當知道其餘的七支：行、識、名色、六處、觸、受、有，也是因也是果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》三唯是因等者：三謂無明、愛、取，發業潤生此為根本，說唯是因。二謂生、老死，樂著戲論及業異熟之所生故，此酬前相，說唯是果。諸所餘支，望義說別，亦因亦果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三是指無明、愛、取，由無明引發造業；由愛取滋潤行、識、名色、六處、觸、受轉成有，能感得生的果報體，無明、愛、取是發業潤生的根本，因此說這三種唯是因。二是指生及老死，由樂著戲論因及淨不淨業因變異成熟之所產生，這是酬答前面無明、愛、取三種因相，說唯是果。其他所餘七支，由其含義說為別支，也是因也是果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　樂著戲論因是無始以來由無明遍計諸法為實所熏習的名言種子，每一生都不斷的熏習，不易覺察，卻是流轉生死數取趣的正因，於生支是親因緣；淨不淨業是由於無明所造的善或不善業，由愛、取滋潤轉成有，是導致取得哪一趣果報的因，於生支及老死支是增上緣，於受生時再由我愛滋潤使這二種因所成的業有現行而有生及老死，所以說生及老死是此無明、愛、取三種因所得之果。佛陀教導眾生應通達諸法實相，破無明、愛、取等煩惱，使名言種子及業種子所成的業有不得煩惱滋潤就沒有生老死，這是出離三界解脫生死的正道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、約獨雜相辨2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科約獨雜相辨，以獨相及雜相所攝說明十二支的次第，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾是獨相？幾是雜相？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：十二有支中哪幾支是屬於不與餘支相交雜的獨相？哪幾支是與餘支相交雜的雜相？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p768"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答2　天一、總標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科總標，總相標示。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：三是獨相，行等是雜相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：只有無明、愛、取三支是獨相，其他行、識、名色、六處、觸、受、有、生、老死，九支都是雜相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》三是獨相等者：三謂無明、愛、取，不與餘支相交雜故，說名獨相。與此相違說名雜相，如行等是。下別問答，其義可知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無明、愛、取是屬於煩惱，不與其他支相交雜，所以是獨相。如果不是獨支，有相交雜的地方，如行等支，就是雜相。下文會各別提出問題及回答，由此可以了解其中的義理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、別辨3　地一、說行有2　玄一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別辨，各別說明，分三科；第一科說行有，說明行與有是雜相所攝，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何故行、有是雜相？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問；為什麼說行、有是雜相？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：由二種說故。謂能引愛非愛果故，及能生趣差別故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：行支與有支由引、生因顯「業」有二種差別說，因此行與有為雜相，一、能引愛非愛果，由行支能引發三界可愛或不愛的果報；二、能生趣差別，由有支能感生五趣不同的果報。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由二種說故等者：行、有二支體非一異，然望義別，是故說二。謂引因位建立行支，由能引愛非愛果故；若生因位建立有支，由近能生五趣差別果故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行支與有支，這二支體性不是同一也不是相異，但是相望其中的法義有差別，因此說是二支。主要是在引因位時建立為行支，是由於能引愛非愛果的緣故；如果是在生因位時建立為有支，是由於有支就近能生五趣的差別果的緣故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行支與有支都有業在其中，但它們也有差別，一個是能引；一個是能生的；它們的體性是同一個但作用不同，一個是引生果報，一個是感生果報。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、說識與名色六處一分2　玄一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科說識與名色六處一分，說明識與名色六處一分有雜相，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何故識與名色、六處一分有雜相？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為什麼識與名色、六處的一分有相雜的情況？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p769"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》識與名色六處一分有雜相者：名色支中，識說為名；六處支中，識說意處；由是故說識與名色、六處一分有雜相義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　名就是受想行識，在名色支中識可以稱為名；在眼耳鼻舌身意六處支中，識是屬於意處，因此說識與名色、六處一分有雜相義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：由三種說故。謂依雜染時故，依潤時故，依轉時故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：由於識在流轉的前後三種時中有不同的功用，因此說識與名色、六處一分有雜相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、依雜染時，有情由無明而發動福等三行，同時熏成隨業識，此時識支被業雜染所染。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷3說：依雜染時是指識支，就是前文所說由邪行故令心顛倒，這是指中有末心名為顛倒，因為能引支（無明緣行）是顛倒故，本識中識支種子隨順能引也名為心顛倒，所以說此時識被邪行的雜染所染；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、依潤時，有情由愛取滋潤使識種子結生相續而有名色，此時識是名色中名的一分，因此依潤生說識與名色一分有相雜義；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、依轉時，流轉中當諸根圓滿時是六處支，識是六處中的意處，因此說識與六處一分有相雜義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由三種說故等者：依雜染時說名識支，謂由邪行令心顛倒。依彼潤時建立名色支，謂識種子愛、取潤已，能取能滿當來名色自體，令住結生相續故；識於其中是其少分，由是說言名色一分。依彼轉時建立六處支，眼等六處圓滿生已，能為眼等六識所依，即於爾時彼眼等識得意處名；識於其中是其少分，由是說言六處一分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依雜染時說名識支，是說由無明發起邪行使心生起顛倒，識被邪行的雜染所染，所以說依雜染時說名識支。當識種子被愛取滋潤時，識種子能取得及能圓滿將來的名色自體，使令識能安住於結生相續的新的名色果報體中，識在名色中是其中的一部分，因此說為名色一分。於識依止六根而轉現時，建立六處支。眼等六處圓滿生長已後，能為眼耳鼻舌身意六識所依止，依根緣境才能發識，這時眼等六識得到意處的名稱；識是意處中的少部分，因此說是六處一分。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地三、說識乃至受與生老死2　玄一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科說識乃至受與生老死，說明識乃至受與生老死有雜相，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何故識乃至受，與生、老死有雜相？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為什麼識、名色、六處、觸、受，與生、老死有雜相？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：由二種說故。謂別顯苦相故，及顯引生差別故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：識、名色、六處、觸、受五支「依別顯苦相」及顯「引、生差别」二種理由，與生、老死二支分別被建立於十二有支中，然體性上並非相異，所以説識乃至受，與生、老死有雜相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、別顯苦相，《瑜伽師地論略纂》卷4說：識乃至受等五支於現行位，能顯苦苦、壞苦、行苦三種苦相，名生老死；若處於種子因位時，苦相還不能顯現，則名為識等五支。約別顯苦相而言，識乃至受等五支是種子之因位苦，生老死是現行之果位苦，所以下文說無明行緣所引識乃至受是苦芽‧‧‧生與老死，當知是苦樹。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、顯引生差別：識乃至受等五支種子為無明緣行二能引支的「所引果」；識乃至受等五支種子於果位時為生老死，生老死為愛取有三支能生因的「所生果」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p770"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由二種說故等者：依有苦因，建立識乃至受支；依有苦果，建立生、老死支。又識乃至受，此於當來為苦；生及老死，此於現法為苦；由是說言別顯苦相。又識乃至受，於現法中引果所攝；生及老死，於後法中生果所攝；由是說言及顯引生差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依止有苦果的因，建立識、名色、六處、觸、受五支；依止所生的苦果，建立生、老死二支。其中的識乃至受五支，是指於將來所感得的果報為苦；生及老死二支，是於現法中為苦；由於在未來世與現在世各有苦相，因此說別顯苦相。在現法中，無明、行二支是能引的因；識乃至受五支是屬於所引果所攝；在後法中，愛、取、有三支是能生的因；生、老死二支是屬於所生果所攝；所以論中說「及顯引生差別」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、緣義分別2　酉一、辨為緣4　戌一、由生已不住義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科緣義分別，說明緣的義理分別，分二科；第一科辨為緣，說明「為緣」的意思，又分四科；第一科由生已不住義，由生已不住義為緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，於緣起中，云何數往義？謂生已不住義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，在十二緣起當中，什麼稱為數往義？就是生了以後，不能停留，一定會繼續再往前，就一定會死，死了以後，只要煩惱繫縛未斷，一定會再生，於是數生數死，生已不住稱為數往義。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以下這一大科可以配合第六科緣起釋詞解讀。這一段文，是緣起釋詞中第一種依字釋名的補充解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》云何數往義等者：前釋詞中說：由煩惱繫縛，往諸趣中數數生起故，名為緣起。今釋彼義，故問答辨。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文說緣起的釋詞依字釋名中解釋：由於煩惱繫縛沒有斷，往五趣中一次又一次的死了又生起五蘊，名為緣起。現在解釋那一段文義，所以用問答說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、由諸緣聚集義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由諸緣聚集義，由諸緣聚集義為緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何和合義？謂諸緣聚集義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是和合義呢？是指眾緣聚集相應義。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　世間因緣所生色心諸法，色法由因緣與增上緣和合而生，心法由因緣、等無間緣、所緣緣、與增上緣和合而生，都是有為法，有生住滅相，而有為法沒有一法是單一緣所生，決定是眾緣和合而生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這一段文，是緣起釋詞中第二種依剎那義的補充解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、由諸緣引攝新新生義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科由諸緣引攝新新生義，說明由諸緣引攝新新生起義為緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何起義？謂諸緣和合之所引攝新新生義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是起義？是指由眾緣相應和合所引攝諸有為法新新生起的道理。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這一段文，是緣起釋詞中第二種依剎那義及第三種依有作用義的補充解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p771"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》云何和合義及起義等者：前釋詞中說：依託眾緣，速謝滅已，續和合生，故名緣起。今釋彼義，故問答辨。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文所解釋文詞中說：依託眾緣聚集法生起，剎那迅速謝滅後，又相續眾緣和合生起，故名為緣起。現在解釋那一段的文義，所以用問答說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌四、由諸行生起法性及現行義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科由諸行生起法性及現行義，說明由諸行生起法性及現行義為緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="44715:7568"></a>云何緣起？云何緣生？謂諸行生起法性，是名緣起；即彼生已，說名緣生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是緣起？什麼是緣生？是指一切有為法，由眾緣和合生起的法性，是名為緣起，所以說：此有故彼有；由緣所生之法生起以後，說名為緣生，所以說：此生故彼生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這一段文，是緣起釋詞中第三種依有作用義及第五種依等覺義的補充解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》云何緣起云何緣生等者：前釋詞中說：眾緣過去而不捨離，乃至此生故彼生，非餘。今釋彼義，故問答辨。當知諸行生起法性，是名緣起，釋此有故彼有；即彼生已，說名緣生，釋此生故彼生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文說到緣起釋詞中說：諸緣生法依託眾緣生現行以後，因已受盡，自性已滅，眾緣過去而不捨離，但並不是謝滅就沒有了，事實上，過去的法生起的同時又在阿賴耶識中熏習了種子，雖經百千劫，假使因緣和合，依於自身相續的阿賴耶識中種子仍會生起現行，能令有情的愛非愛果異熟成熟，所以如佛所說：此有故彼有，此生故彼生，由此可知諸法並不是無因而生或如二乘說由無為而生或如外道說由常法而生。現在解釋緣起釋詞的義理，所以用問答說明。應當知道一切有為法，由眾緣和合生起的法性，是名緣起，這是解釋此有故彼有；而由緣所生之法生起以後，說名為緣生，是解釋此生故彼生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、明彼攝2　戌一、苦諦攝2　亥一、現法為苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明彼攝，說明十二支為苦集二諦所攝，分二科；第一科苦諦攝，說明苦諦所攝支，又分二科；第一科現法為苦，說明現法為苦的諸支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾支苦諦攝，及現法為苦？答：二，謂生及老死。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：十二緣起中有哪幾支是屬於苦諦，以及現在生命體就是苦？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：二支，指生及老死支是苦諦所攝而且是現法為苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、當來為苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科當來為苦，說明當來為苦的諸支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾支苦諦攝，當來為苦？答：識乃至受種子性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：十二支中幾支是苦諦所攝，幾支是將來為苦？答：五支是苦諦所攝當來為苦，識乃至受這五法種子是苦諦所攝，而且是將來感得果報後才現行成苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、集諦攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科集諦攝，說明集諦所攝支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾支集諦攝？答：所餘支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：十二支中幾支是集諦所攝？答：除了識乃至受生及老死所餘支包括無明、行、愛、取、有的五支，惑、業都是屬於集諦所攝。這裡沒有說滅諦和道諦，因為滅道二諦是還滅的緣起，不是流轉的緣起，所以十二緣起支只說苦諦與集諦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p772"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、十二支前後相望分別2　酉一、辨為緣2　戌一、前支是後支緣2　亥一、唯望近支2　天一、明次第6　地一、無明望行2　玄一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科十二支前後相望分別，十二支中前支與後支互相對望的分別，分二科；第一科辨為緣，說明諸支互相為緣的情況，又分二科；第一科前支是後支緣，說明前支一定是後支的緣，又分二科；第一科唯望近支，只有相對於最近的一支，又分二科；第一科明次第，說明其中的次第，又分六科；第一科無明望行，以無明與行相對來說，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="3685:7578"></a>問：無明與行為作俱有緣？為作無間滅緣？為作久遠滅緣？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：無明對行而言是行的俱有緣？或作無間滅緣？或作久遠滅緣？兩支一起活動稱為俱有緣，無間滅緣就是前一法謝滅，為後一法無間生起的緣，如有了無明生起以後，沒有間斷即有行的造作及行的種子熏習到阿賴識中；久遠滅緣是指過去的業行雖久遠已謝滅，但於過去造作業行時所熏習的種子，遇到生緣時就會生起現行感得果報。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、答2　黃一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標，標出三緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：當知具作三緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：應該知道無明對行來說為俱有緣、無間滅緣、久遠滅緣三種緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、釋3　宇一、為俱有覆障緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科為俱有覆障緣，說明無明是行的俱有覆障緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂由無知，於隨順諸行法中，為俱有覆障緣，為彼彼事發起諸行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於無知，就是無明，在隨順種種的福行、非福行、不動行的法中，無明於造業時是同時俱有覆障心識去認識真實相的緣，為了各式各樣的事情就會造作福行、非福行、或不動行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂由無知至發起諸行者：此中諸行，通說身語意三非福與福及不動行。由說無明與行作俱有緣故，色無色行俱有轉故。諸有現前愛非愛境，此能隨順造非福行；於死及生起決定信，求可愛生，此能隨順造諸福行；於色無色有過患身起功德想，此能隨順造不動行；如是等類，是名隨順行法。於此諸法由無知故令不顯了，是故無明與行能作俱有覆障緣。由覆障故，不知過患、不知出離，依三界愛，或無有愛，造作非福、福行、或不動行，是名為彼彼事發起諸行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡的諸行通說身語意三行所造作的非福、福及不動行。由於無明與行作俱有緣的同時，無色的意行與色法的身語行是一起活動的。現前面對可愛的境界和不可愛的境界時，由於無明俱行而生貪瞋，會隨順去造非福行的種種的罪惡錯誤的行為；對於會死亡與還有下一生這件事生起決定的信心，承認有因果輪迴，為追求下一生可愛的生命體，就會去造諸福行。例如對佛菩薩常供花就會使來生長得很莊嚴，對於色界與無色界中有過患沒有解脫的果報身生起有功德想，就會去造禪定的不動業；這些由無明所覆障造作的業行，名為隨順行法。對於這些所造作事由於無知的原因，使令自己不明白世出世間的因果，因此無明對行能作為同時俱有的覆障緣。由於心識被無明覆障的原因，不知道有過患、不知道應該出離，依止對三界的愛著，或是無有愛，而造作非福、福行、或不動行，是名於彼彼事發起諸行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《攝大乘論抄》卷1：緣果報斷滅生愛，名無有愛。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷5說：有情不了解涅槃由煩惱滅而得，而執著此身斷滅則是涅槃，於是計度執著自身到此無有，愛身無有，名無有愛。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《阿毘達磨集異門足論》卷4說：欣樂無有的有情，於無有中諸貪等貪，執藏防護耽著愛染，名無有愛。例如有一類有情為怖畏所逼、怖畏所惱、憂苦所逼、憂苦所惱，苦受所觸，因此這樣想：如何當來令我身死後斷壞無有，永絕眾病，豈不是非常快樂嗎。這類有情欣樂無有，於無有中生起諸貪等貪，執藏防護耽著愛染，因此名無有愛。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有情若有三界的有愛及無有愛都會生起貪瞋癡而造業，所以佛說：「愛所執有情，心貪有無有，魔軛所軛故，身常不安樂。流轉諸有中，生已歸老死，如犢子愛乳，隨母嘗不離。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p773"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇二、為無間滅生起緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科為無間滅生起緣，說明無明是行的無間滅生起緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又由惡見、放逸俱行無知，為無間滅生起緣，發起諸行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由於有惡見、有放逸俱行的無知，由無明引發無間滅生起緣，發起種種的業行（意行）。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又由惡見至發起諸行者：此中諸行，唯意所攝非福與福及不動行，由說無明為無間滅緣故，唯望無色有此緣故。於三世內外諸行，及於因所生法，起不如理分別，是名惡見。於業異熟及俱，不能思擇諸行過失，是名放逸。此與無知同行相應，是名俱行。由是無明差別，說有見愚及放逸愚。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/09.htm#7587:6971">陵本九卷十八頁712</a>）由此無知，前無間滅，後決定生，故說與行為無間滅生起緣，由是發起諸無色行。</span></strong></span></span></p>
