<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡所說的諸行，唯是由意業所攝的非福、福、及不動行，由無明覆障為無間滅生起緣，只有無色的心行才有這種無間滅緣。對於過去現在未來三世由於內五蘊及外境的諸有為法，及於因緣所生法，生起不如理的分別，名為惡見。對於業行、異熟果及業行與異熟果的因果關係，不能思惟簡擇所造作的身語意行的過失，名為放逸。這些心識與無知同行相應，是名俱行。由這些無明的差別，說有種種的惡見愚癡及放逸的愚癡。在〈有尋有伺等三地〉卷9，298頁有說過見愚和放逸愚。由於這類無知，前法的無明無間滅，後法的業行決定生起，所以說無明與行是無間滅生起緣，因此發起種種無色的心行，進一步由意發動身語的造作。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇三、為久遠滅引發緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科為久遠滅引發緣，說明無明與行為久遠滅引發緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又由無知，為久遠滅引發緣故，建立順彼當生相續。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由於無明過去引發所造的業行，當時就在識中熏習下業種子，業行雖久遠已滅，由於無明沒有斷除，識中的種子遇到愛取的滋潤，還是能建立隨順將生的果報相續，所以說無明為行的久遠滅引發緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又由無知至當生相續者：如前已說，設彼無明不永斷者，依於識等受最為後所有諸行後際應生。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/09.htm#7590:6841">陵本九卷十五頁695</a>）是故無明既發業已，雖久遠滅，然說為緣，能引當生自相續身，以是隨順因故，由此建立為引發緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前面已經說過，假設無明沒有永遠斷除，所依止的識、名色、六處、觸、受五法種子受到愛取的滋潤，下一世五蘊的果報就會生起。如〈有尋有伺等三地〉卷9，286頁中所說。因此過去由無明發動造業，當時在識中熏下業種子，業行雖久遠已滅，然而識中的種子遇到愛取的滋潤為緣，能引發將要生起的自體相續五蘊果報，這是由於無明煩惱未斷的隨順因所生，由此建立為引發緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p774"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、行望識等2　玄一、舉行望識2　黃一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科行望識等，說明行支對望識支等的關係，分二科；第一科舉行望識，舉出行支望識支，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：云何應知諸行望識為三種緣？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如何應該知道諸行望識為三種緣？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、答3　宇一、為俱有緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科為俱有緣，說明諸行望識為俱有緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：由能熏發彼種子故，為俱有緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：由於造作業行能同時熏發識的種子，作為識的俱有緣。每當福行非福行和不動行一發動，馬上熏下識乃至受五法的種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇二、為無間滅生起緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科為無間滅生起緣，說明諸行望識為無間滅生起緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">次後由彼勢力轉故，為無間滅生起緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，由業行熏發識的種子以後，隨業識由行的勢力令次念識種生起，能為後有相續果識的無間滅生起緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇三、為久遠滅引發緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科為久遠滅引發緣，說明諸行望識為久遠滅引發緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由彼當來果得生故，為久遠滅引發緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於過去所造業種子可使將來的果報識得以生起，是識的久遠滅引發緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》諸行望識為三種緣等者：行能熏發彼識種子，能熏所熏俱生俱滅，由是說名為俱有緣。從此以後，此識名隨業識，隨業勢力乃至命終流轉不絕，能為後有相續識因，由是說為無間滅生起緣。復由諸行為牽引因，當來識果方可得生，即此說為久遠滅引發緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　業行能熏發識的種子，能熏的業行及所熏的識種是俱生俱滅，同在一起活動也一起消滅，稱為俱有緣。從此以後，此識就有業隨逐稱為隨業識，隨著業的力量乃至命終，識乃至受這五法的種子都會一直隨識相續流轉不絕，能做為後有相續識的因，因此說為無間滅生起緣。又由於各個所造的業行為牽引因，將來識的果報才可以得生，由此說為久遠滅引發緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、例識望名色等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例識望名色等，例舉識望名色等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p775"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如行望識，如是識望名色、名色望六處、六處望觸、觸望受亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同行望識，因此識望名色、名色望六處、六處望觸、觸望受也是一樣有三種緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如行望識至觸望受亦爾者：當知此中，名色、六處、觸、受種子皆為諸行同時熏發，非離諸行一一相望有次第別，唯依當來現起分位有次第故，說彼因性亦有次第。由是道理，識望名色等說為三種緣者，意顯行熏識已，名色、六處、觸、受種子為識攝受，不離於識別有因性，從識為熏，故言亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應該知道在造業同時名色、六處、觸、受種子都與識被種種的業行同時熏發，並不是遠離所造諸行一支一支相望有次第的差別，其實是同時熏發成五法種子，其中唯依將來在母胎中果報現起的分位，有名色為先、六根成長、能生觸、而有受等次第的差別，而說在因性也有次第差別。由於這個道理，識相對於名色說有三種緣者，意思是顯示行在熏識時，名色六入觸受的種子，是由識所攝受的，不能離開識另外有名色等因性存在，都是熏到識中，所以說亦爾。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地三、受望愛2　玄一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科受望愛，說明受支與愛支的關係，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：云何應知受望愛為三種緣？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：怎麼樣可以知道受相對於愛是愛的三種緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、答3　黃一、為俱有緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科為俱有緣，說明受望愛為俱有緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：當知由彼起樂著故，為俱有緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：應當知道現行受同時生起愛味執著的緣故，說受望愛為俱有緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由彼起樂著故為俱有緣者：由彼樂受起和合愛，由彼苦受起別離愛，以於自體境界受中貪味繫縛故，總說樂著名。依此建立為俱有緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於樂受會生起繼續受樂的和合愛，對苦受會生起快一點遠離的別離愛，因為於自體受與境界受中有貪的愛味繫縛的緣故，總說為「樂著」的名稱。受和愛是同時稱為俱有緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、為無間滅生起緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科為無間滅生起緣，說明受望愛為無間滅生起緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p776"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">從此無間，由彼勢力起追求等作用轉故，為無間滅生起緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於現行受有和合愛或者別離愛以後，從此沒有無間斷由受俱愛的力量而追求或遠離各種境界的作用轉現，使愛剎那滅又剎那生，因此說受是愛的無間滅生起緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》從此無間至生起緣者：由彼樂受起和合愛，從此無間，故起追求；由彼苦受起別離愛，從此無間，故起厭離；是名追求等作用轉。依此說為無間滅生起緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於樂受生起和合愛，從此沒有間斷，由愛的力量就會開始追求；由於接觸苦受時就生起別離愛，接著沒有間斷就會產生厭離，追求遠離，名為追求等作用轉。依此道理說受是愛的無間滅生起緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃三、為久遠滅引發緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科為久遠滅引發緣，說明受望愛為當來相續久遠滅引發緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">建立當來難可解脫彼相續故，為久遠滅引發緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於無明觸所生受為所依止生愛已滅，雖經久遠，能建立將來難可解脫由愛使果報相續的力量，所以說受為愛的久遠滅引發緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》建立當來至引發緣者：謂由無明觸所生受為依止故，貪愛得生，當來相續難可解脫。依此說為久遠滅引發緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於無明觸所生受為所依止，貪愛得以生起，將來的生命體還會再相續，依這種道理說為久遠滅引發緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地四、愛望取2　玄一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科愛望取，說明愛支與取支的關係，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：云何愛望取為三種緣？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：怎麼樣說愛望取有三種緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、答3　黃一、為俱有緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科為俱有緣，說明愛望取為俱有緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：由欲貪俱行，於隨順取法中，欲樂安立故，為俱有緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：由取時心與欲貪俱行，於隨順四種取法中，都有欲望愛樂的貪愛及於所安立我語的貪愛為諸取的因緣故，有取時一定有愛同時活動，所以說愛望取為俱有緣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷3說：愛與能取（於欲、見、戒禁、我語四種欲貪名能取）實際上並不同時，但依所取之欲、見、戒禁、我語，所為取如為得諸欲及為受用而生欲取等之因緣與愛俱有，所以說愛望取成俱有緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p777"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由欲貪俱行至為俱有緣者：欲貪俱行是其能取，隨順取法是其所取，欲樂安立是所為取。由欲樂故起前三取，由安立故起第四取。如是一切俱有而轉，由是故說為俱有緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲貪與心同時活動是能取，隨順生起取的欲、見、戒禁、我語是所取，取的欲樂及安立是所為取，就是指生起取的動機，如為得諸欲及為受用而生欲取；由貪利養及以恭敬增上力故，或為詰責他所立論，或為免脫他所難，起第二見取；由奢摩他支為所依止，為所建立，為欲往趣世間離欲乃至非想非非想處三摩鉢底，起第三戒禁取；為欲隨說分別所計作業受果所有士夫，及為隨說流轉還滅士夫之相，起我語取。由於心中的欲樂而生起欲、見、戒禁前三取，由安立故起我語的第四取。如是一切諸取都有愛的煩惱俱時而起，因此說愛是取的俱有緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、為無間滅生起緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科為無間滅生起緣，說明愛望取為無間滅生起緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由無間滅勢力轉故，為生起緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於愛的力量前一念滅，後一念就會有取，所以說愛是取的無間滅生起緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃三、為久遠滅引發緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三為久遠滅引發緣，說明愛望取為當來久遠滅引發緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">建立當來難可解脫彼相續故，為久遠滅引發緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有了愛就會推動取，取滅之後，久遠之後，遇緣愛取現行仍能引發以前由業行熏習的種子，使令行、識、名色、六處、觸、受等六支形成有支，生起難可解脫的果報，所以說愛望取為當來久遠滅引發緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地五、取望有2　玄一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科取望有，說明取支與有支的關係，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：云何取望有為三種緣？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為什麼取望有為三種緣？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、答3　黃一、為俱有緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科為俱有緣，說明取望有為俱有緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：由與彼俱，令業能招諸趣果故，為俱有緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：由於取的煩惱活動使過去的業行種子結合識、名色、六處、觸、受五法種子生起現行為有，與取在一起，使業有能招感得所對應諸趣的果報，所以說取為有的俱有緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由與彼俱至為俱有緣者：異熟識中先所積集行等種子，為取攝受，轉名為有，依此義故，說與彼俱，是故建立為俱有緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　現法的異熟果報識中先前所積集的行、識、名色、六處、觸、受等種子，被取所攝受，使這六法種子同時生起現行，轉名為有，依這個道理，說取與有在一起，因此建立取為有的俱有緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、為無間滅生起緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科為無間滅生起緣，說明取望有為無間滅生起緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p778"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又由彼力，於此生處能引識等故，為無間滅生起緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由取煩惱的力量使令過去的業行種子結合識、名色、六處、觸、受五法種子無間生起現行，這就是取為有的無間滅生起緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又由彼力至生起緣者：由彼取力，能令生有將入現在，於此諸趣所當生處，能引識乃至受自體果生，依此說為無間滅生起緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於取的力量，能使令生有將會進入到現在，當中有將隨業識帶到五趣受生處，由取俱有能引發識、名色、六處、觸、受的自體異熟果生起，依此說取為有的無間滅生起緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃三、為久遠滅引發緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科為久遠滅引發緣，說明取望有為久遠滅引發緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又能引發彼界功能故，為久遠滅引發緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由取能引發過去的業行所熏等種子成為有的功能，從最初造業熏種到感果，經過很久，仍能引發種子現行，所以說取為有的久遠滅引發緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又能引發彼界功能等者：先所積集行等種子，是名彼界功能。由取攝受，漸令增長，名能引發。從其最初為隨順因，依此說為久遠滅引發緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　過去所積集熏習的行、識、名色、六處、觸、受六法的種子，這些種子又稱為界或稱為因，名為彼界功能。由取攝受使令這些種子逐漸的增長，名為能引發。從最初的無明緣行所積集的行等種子，由「取」為隨順因，引發行等種子現行轉成為「有」，依此說取為有的久遠滅引發緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地六、有望生生望老死2　玄一、正辨二支為緣2　黃一、舉有望生2　宇一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科有望生生望老死，說明有望生生望老死，分二科；第一科正辨二支為緣，說明二支為緣，又分二科；第一科舉有望生，舉出有望生，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：云何有望生為三種緣？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為什麼業有相對於生支來說是三種緣？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇二、答3　宙一、為俱有緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科為俱有緣，說明有望生為俱有緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：熏發彼種子故，為俱有緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：有的同時就有生的種子，由取使令行、識、名色、六處、觸、受轉成為有，被愛取滋潤的有支熏發識等名言種子令生現行，所以有望生為俱有緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宙二、為無間滅生起緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科為無間滅生起緣，說明有望生為無間滅生起緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由彼勢力無間隨轉故，為生起緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於有支的力量能為生現行的等無間緣，所以說有望生為無間滅生起緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p779"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宙三、為久遠滅引發緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科為久遠滅引發緣，說明有望生為久遠滅引發緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">雖久遠滅而果轉故，為引發緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又行、識乃至受六法種子（有支）雖然已滅，久遠以後由愛取滋資潤有支現行能使生支的果報相續生起，因此有支望生支為引發緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》有望生為三種緣等者：有所攝種功能現前，能生後有，即初剎那有望於生，說為俱有緣。次後由彼勢力相續隨轉，說為無間滅生起緣。有為生因，生是彼果，生因現行雖久遠滅，而生因果自體得生，依此說為引發緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有支所攝持的行、識、名色、六處、觸、受種子功能現前，能生起後有果報，於最初剎那的有支望於生支是同時，投生那一剎那有與生是同時在一起，說為俱有緣。次剎那後由於有支勢力，使生支相續隨轉，說為無間滅生起緣。有支是生支的因，生支是有支的果，生因的業行雖久遠已滅，而業有所攝的識乃至受種子遇愛取滋潤仍可生起現行，使得生因的果報自體得生，依此說有支為生支的久遠滅引發緣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若據《瑜伽論記》卷3：「雖久遠滅而果轉者，如初潤有望初生，果轉故成久遠滅引發緣，隔正死時故。」也就是隔一生所以稱作「久遠」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、例生望老死</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例生望老死，例說生望老死的緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如有望生，當知生望老死為緣亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同有支望生支，應該知道生支望老死支為俱有等三種緣也是如此。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如有望生等者：由有生故，老死隨逐；從生為言，故說亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於有生的時候，以生為緣，同時有老死隨逐；老死與生支都是以識乃至受五法種子為體，從生支說也具三緣，因此說亦爾。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於生時，能熏發老死的種子，故說生為老死的俱有緣；由生的勢力無間有老死隨轉，因此說生為老死的無間滅生起緣；生為老死的因，老死是生的果，老死與生都以識乃至受五法種子為體，依識乃至受五法種子現行的分位差別而假安立為生或老死，引發老死的因（識乃至受五法種子）雖然已滅，久遠之後遇緣，若由愛取滋潤有，使「生」現行後，能引發老死，所以說生為老死的久遠滅引發緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、兼釋有支建立2　黃一、略標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科兼釋有支建立，解釋有支的建立，分二科；第一科略標，要略標出二種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，建立有支有二種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，建立有支有二種解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、列釋2　宇一、勝分建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列釋，列舉出來解釋，分二科；第一科勝分建立，說明依有支中的勝分建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、就勝分建立，謂取所攝受業，如前已說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、由業有力量感果，因此說就勝分建立「有支」。就勝分建立此處業有是指由取滋潤長養的福、非福等「業」有，如前面已說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　再詳細說，識、名色、六入、觸、受五法種子，雖能為正因，不名有的原故，即識等五果名言種子雖望當來生老現行是正因緣，若不得業感必無力能生自果，故說業種名有支，不說識等五果名有支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p780"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂取所攝受如前已說者：謂如前說，煩惱滋長故，發起愛非愛業。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/10.htm#7657:7280">陵本十卷三頁741</a>）當知唯就勝分建立，說取緣有。今此義同，故置如前。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前面所說，因為有煩惱的滋潤長養，而熏發可愛果或不可愛果的業因轉成有，如本卷307頁所說。應該知道取緣有唯是以力量比較強的業來建立。這也就是取所攝受的業稱為有，所以說如前已說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇二、全分建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科全分建立，依有支整體的內涵建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、全分建立，謂業及識乃至受所有種子，取所攝受，建立為有應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、全分有的內容是業，及識、名色、六處、觸、受所有的種子合有六法，六法為取所攝受時，建立為「有」應當知道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、顯業用2　地一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二顯業用，顯示十二支的業用，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：是諸有支唯有次第與行為緣乃至老死，更有餘業用耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：這十二有支是只有次第與行為緣乃至與老死為緣，只有前支為後支的增上緣，或是還有其他的作用呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》是諸有支至更有餘業用者：十二有支，從初無明乃至最後老死，前為後緣，漸次相稱，當知唯依增上緣說。今此問意，謂諸有支，為唯如是一增上緣耶？為更有餘緣業用耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十二有支，從初無明支乃至最後老死支，前支為後支緣，漸次相稱，應該知道唯是依增上緣而說的。現在提出問題，這十二有支，只是前支為後支的增上緣嗎？或是還有其他緣的業用？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：即此業用，及於各別所行境中，如其所應所有業用，當知是名第二業用。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：除了前支為後支的增上緣業用，還有諸支自種現行的因緣業用與其他諸支相應的所有業用，以前支與後支相望來說，前面說過無色支望無色支有三種緣，望有色支是只有增上緣，有色支望無色支二種緣就是所緣緣和增上緣，望有色支只有增上緣。除增上緣以外，所有其他業用稱為第二業用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p781"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》即此業用至第二業用者：此諸支自體種子生自現行，是名因緣業用。及與餘支相望，於各別所行境中，或為無色，或為有色，如其所應，為等無間緣、所緣緣及增上緣。如是業用差別，前緣性中已具顯示。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/10.htm#7666:7374">陵本十卷五頁751</a>）如是所說緣義業用，當知是名第二業用。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這十二有支的各支自體種子為因緣，生起自己支的現行，名為因緣業用。及前支與所餘支相望，於各別所行境界中，有的是無色，有的是有色，如色法與無色法能為所緣緣及增上緣或無色法能為無色法的等無間緣、所緣緣及增上緣，無色法與有色法能為增上緣。這些業用差別，在前面的緣性中已經都已說明顯示。如本卷311頁所說。因緣等業用，在前面的緣性時已完全顯示。這類的緣的業用稱為第二業用。 （連結：<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/C10-01.htm">十二有支諸支二種業用</a>）</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、亦望餘支2　天一、舉無明2　地一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科亦望餘支，相對於其他支的緣，分二科；第一科舉無明，舉無明支說，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：無明唯與行為緣，亦與餘支為緣耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：無明只給行支作緣嗎？還是也給其他支作緣呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、答2　玄一、通一切</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科通一切，說明無明通一切支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="7712:7670"></a>答：無明乃至亦與老死為緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：無明影響最深，可以染污其他十一支，可以給行乃至老死作緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、會前說</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科會前說，會同前面所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前言唯與行為緣者，但說近緣義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面只說無明緣行只有給予行做緣，這只是以最近的緣來說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、例所餘</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例所餘，例說其餘。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是所餘盡應當知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其他所餘支，如無明也可以給識作緣，由有無明生行才有生死流轉的阿賴耶識，如是前前支能予後後支為緣的道理也一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由前面所說一支一支之間都有俱有緣，依此可以解釋一剎那俱有十二緣起。一剎那間具足無明乃至老死。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無間滅緣是有次第的十二緣起，前一剎那滅後一剎那生，次第來說十二緣起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　久遠滅緣則是說過去的業行所熏的種子因當來遇緣得果而生死流轉，依有因就會得果說十二緣起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由思惟十二緣起支可以了知生死流轉與還滅的要義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、後支非前支緣4　亥一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科後支非前支緣，後支不是前支的緣，分四科；第一科標，標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，後支非前支緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，後支不是前支的緣。行對無明來說行不是無明的緣，乃至老死對生來說老死不是生的緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提出問題。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼這麼說？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p782"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如為斷後支故，勤作功用斷於前支，由前斷故，後亦隨斷。非為斷前故，勤作功用斷於後支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果要斷後支，努力精勤修習止觀斷於前支，由於前支斷，後支也隨之而斷。並不是為斷前支，而努力精勤修習止觀去斷後支。因為前支是後支的緣，前支斷了，後支沒有緣，自然斷而不起。例如要斷行一定要斷無明，努力的修行斷除前支，前支斷掉下一支就沒有緣了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥四、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故當知唯此為彼緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所以應該知道前支一定是後支的緣，斷了前支，後支自然斷。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如為斷後支故等者：此中道理，應知如緣起聖道經說。彼云：由誰有故而有老死？如是老死復由何緣？我於此事如理思時，便生如是如實現觀：由有生故便有老死，如是老死由生為緣，如是廣說乃至齊識退還。即此中說為斷後支，勤作功用斷於前支。又云：我復思惟：無有誰故而無老死？由誰滅故老死隨滅？我即於此如理思時，便生如是如實現觀：無有生故便無老死，由生滅故老死隨滅，如是廣說乃至無明滅故行即隨滅。即此中說由前斷故，後亦隨斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這其中的道理，應當知道如《緣起聖道經》說：由誰先有而會有老死？老死是什麼緣為因才有？佛陀如理思惟這件事時，就生起如諸法實相的現量觀慧：有生命體一定會有老死，老死是因為有生才會有老死，這樣一直倒著推想回去，由誰有故有老死，乃至推到識就不需要再往上推，稱為齊識退還。有情去投胎的時候就是識，所以齊識退還到那裡就不用再推想下去了。這就是此處所說為了斷後支，努力精勤修行斷於前支的道理。佛陀又思惟：沒有誰就沒有老死，那一個法滅了老死就會滅呢？這樣如理思惟時就生起如實的現量觀慧：沒有生命體就沒有老死，生滅老死也滅，詳細逆推乃至無明滅故行即隨滅。這就是此處所說只要將前支斷掉，後支就隨著斷除的道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p783"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、釋義別2　戌一、由順觀2　亥一、釋此有故彼有</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋義別，解釋義理上的差別，分二科；第一科由順觀，由順次第觀察，又分二科；第一科釋此有故彼有，解釋此有故彼有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：云何說言此有故彼有？答：由未斷緣，餘得生義故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為什麼說此有故彼有？答：因為沒有斷除諸法的因緣等緣，諸法就可以生出現行。如沒有斷無明種子，無明能生現行，以無明為緣，其餘行乃至老死都能現行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《大乘阿毘達磨雜集論》卷4〈1 三法品〉說：此有故彼有者，顯無作緣生義，唯由有緣故果法得有，但緣沒有真實作用能生果法。《法華經玄贊要集》卷29說：這也是對治外道的邪見而說，如順世外道，計執有情都由四大、父母、極微而生，四大及父母極微有真實作用能生有情，名為作用。又如數論、勝論師計執我為作者，我能為生死之因，我有實作用，現在破斥外道執著四大父母極微、及我有實作用能生有情，說十二支各別從種生，因緣而有，無實作用，無作緣生。此外聲聞乘說一切有部主張十二有支有實作用，此處顯示無作緣生，十二支相望雖有作用，作用無真實自性，唯依如幻諸行假立，因此說無作緣生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由未斷緣餘得生義故者：種子不斷，名未斷緣；現行法生，名餘得生。當知此約緣起義釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果沒有斷除種子，名為未斷緣；現行法一定會生起，名為餘得生。應當知道這是依緣起的道理解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋此生故彼生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋此生故彼生，解釋此生故彼生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：云何此生故彼生？答：由無常緣，餘得生義故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為什麼說此生故彼生？答：由無常的緣為因，能生出其他的無常法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《法華經玄贊要集》卷29說：此生故彼生，是顯無常緣生，無明生故，方行支生，無明若不生，行支也不生，能生都是無常法，這是破聲聞乘大眾部義，以無為為體生出緣生法，及外道常計論，如外道妄執，梵王冥性神我等體是常不從因生，而能為因生其他果法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由無常緣餘得生義故者：諸法自體從自種生，名無常緣，此說生起無常。由此為緣，後支法生，名餘得生。當知此約緣生義釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　諸法的自體從自己的種子生時稱為無常緣，這是說生起無常。由此所生起法為緣，後支法即可生起，名為餘得生。應當知道這是依緣生義做的解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、由逆觀2　亥一、釋要由生緣而有老死等2　天一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由逆觀，由逆次第觀察，分二科；第一科釋要由生緣而有老死等，解釋要由生緣而有老死等，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何故說言有生故有老死，要由生緣而有老死，如是乃至無明望行？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為什麼說有生就有老死，要由生緣而有老死，乃至為什麼有無明所以有行？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：由此言教道理，顯從無實作用緣，餘得生義故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：由於佛開示教導的道理，顯示由有緣故果法得有，非任何單一緣有真實作用，能生能作餘果法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p784"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》顯從無實作用緣餘得生義故者：如有頌言：諸行皆剎那，住尚無況用，即說彼生起，為用為作者。又言：法不能生他，亦不能自生，眾緣有故生，非故新新有。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/16.htm#7697:13585">陵本十六卷七頁1390</a>）如是前支為後支緣，但由勢用為緣，無實作用，道理亦爾。由剎那滅義，無動作義，是緣起義故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如〈思所成地〉勝義伽陀說：這一切有為法都是剎那生、剎那滅，要它安住一段時間都沒有辦法，何況說它有真實作用？可是這如幻如化的境界生起以後，還是要以名言來安立說這就是作用，這就是造業的人，這是假安立的。又說：任何一法不能生出其他的法，也不能自己生出自法，自不能生、他也不能生，眾緣聚集時法就生了，所生出來的法每一剎那都不是舊的而是新的，每一剎那都不一樣，如〈思所成地〉卷16，586頁所說。如是前支為後支緣唯是諸緣勢力的作用，沒有單一法有真實的作用能生諸法，道理也是一樣。由剎那生即剎那滅的義理，可知沒有一法真實從此到彼，所以說無動作義，是緣起義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋非離生緣而有老死等2　天一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋非離生緣而有老死等，解釋非離生緣而有老死等，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何故說言有生故有老死，非離生緣而有老死，如是乃至無明望行？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為什麼說有生故有老死，不是離開生緣而有老死，如是乃至不是離開了無明而會有行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：由此言教道理，顯從自相續緣；即自相續，餘得生義故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：由這裡的言教道理，顯示從自相續緣，就是生命體能繼續相續的緣，其他的法就能夠生出來；依止自身果報體相續，還會造業而有其他的生死輪迴出現。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》顯從自相續緣等者：如前已說，於離作用復因果相續不斷義，是緣起義。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/09.htm#7702:6882">陵本九卷十六頁701</a>）當知唯依諸支相望，漸次相稱，前為後緣，建立因果體性。今義亦爾，故作是說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面已說雖然諸緣沒有真實的作用，可是如幻如化的因果還是相續不斷義，這是緣起義。如〈有尋有伺等三地〉卷9，289頁所說。應當知道這唯是依止前後支相望，漸漸依次第相應相稱，前支為後支的緣，建立因緣果的體性。現在這裡的義理也是如此，因此這樣說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申四、十二支為緣決擇分別2　酉一、依四句答3　戌一、無明與行2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科十二支為緣決擇分別，以四句及順後句決斷簡擇十二支，分二科；第一科依四句答，依四句答決擇十二支分別，又分三科；第一科無明與行，說明無明與行這二支，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若法無明為緣，彼法是行耶？設是行者，彼無明為緣耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如果法是無明為緣，所生的法是行嗎？若是行，是無明為緣嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》中窺基大師說此處不一定是討論十二有支。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以問答的方式，來討論佛法的道理，有很多種方法，有作四句答、順前句、順後句，一行、無事句等。此處說四句答，有時二法的範圍不一定，互有寬狹，於所問應作四句。以A、B，表示二法，第一句是：是A非B；第二句是：是B非A；第三句是：是A也是B；第四句是：非A也非B。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答2　天一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標，標出四句。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p785"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：應作四句。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：應該可以做四句來回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨，說明這四句話。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有行非無明為緣，謂無漏及無覆無記身語意行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一句：或有一種行不是無明為緣，這是指無漏思及無覆無記行即無記思（無覆無記）的身語意行都不是無明為緣，十二支中行支無明唯與有漏業善惡行為緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂無漏及無覆無記身語意行者：此中身語意行，通說無漏及與無覆無記二種應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡所說的身語意行，通於說無漏的戒定慧等身語意行與無覆無記這二種應該知道。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無覆無記據《佛光大辭典》載：無覆無記為「有覆無記」之對稱，又作無覆、淨無記。若以道德之性質為準則，一切諸法可大別為善、惡、無記等三大類。其中，無記係指非善非不善，不能記為善業或惡業之法，又可分為有覆與無覆兩種。無覆無記，即指不覆障聖道的非善非惡之法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　據《俱舍論》卷七、《俱舍論光記》卷七、《法宗源》卷本等所載，無覆無記可分為有為與無為二類：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、有為無記，即由因緣造作所生之無記法，更分為五種，即：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 異熟無記，又作異熟生，為由過去善、不善之因所生之異熟果體；以其不覆障聖道，故為無覆無記。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 威儀無記，又作威儀路心，指行、住、坐、臥等四威儀；因其以色、香、味、觸等四處為體，故其性無記。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3. 工巧無記，又作工巧處心，有身工巧、語工巧二種。刻鏤等之身工巧，以色、香、味、觸等四處為體；歌詠等之語工巧，以色、聲、香、味、觸等五處為體，其性皆為無記。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　4. 通果無記，又作變化無記，指天眼、天耳二種神通自在及其變化；以色、香、味、觸等四處為體，其性亦為無記。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　5. 自性無記，即前四種以外其餘一切無記性之有為法皆稱為自性無記。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、無為無記，即非由因緣造作所生之無記法，亦稱勝義無記，例如三無為中之非擇滅無為及虛空等，皆屬於無為無記。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其中異熟、威儀、工巧、通果等四無記心，欲界之無覆無記皆具有，色界具有除工巧無記以外之其餘三項，無色界則僅有異熟無記一種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又於四無記心中，異熟無記能攀緣六根、六境等十二處而起作用，威儀、工巧、通果等三無記能攀緣色、香、味、觸等四處而起作用，而工巧無記中之語工巧無記及通果無記也能攀緣聲處而起作用，因此也遍通於色、聲、香、味、觸等五境。這裡所說的無覆無記可以參考此處所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或無明為緣而非是行，謂除行所攝有支所餘有支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或者有一種情況，就是無明為緣，可是不是行。是指行以外，其他的識、名色、六入、觸、受、愛、取、有、生、老死的十支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂除行所攝有支所餘有支者：如前已說，無明乃至亦與老死為緣，如是所餘盡應當知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/10.htm#7712:7670">陵本十卷十頁781</a>）是故作如是說。謂與識等乃至老死為緣，名所餘支。餘隨所應，準此應釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前文已說，無明除了行支以外，與所有其餘的十支為緣，應該知道。如本卷324頁所說，因此這樣說。前文說無明與識等乃至老死為緣，名為所餘支。餘支都與無明相應，應準照此種解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有亦無明為緣亦是行，謂福、非福、不動身語意行。除如是相，是第四句。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三句是：或有也是無明為緣也是行，這是指福行、非福行、不動身語意行。除了前三種相，就是非無明亦非是行，非十二有支，如外稼成熟門、器世間成壞門、食任持門、威勢門、清淨門，這是第四句。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、行與識等2　亥一、舉行與識2　天一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科行與識等，決擇行與識等四句的關連，分二科；第一科舉行與識，舉出行與識，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若行為緣，彼亦識耶？設是識者，行為緣耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如果是行為緣，種種的福行、非福行、不動行一定能生識嗎？如果是識，一定是行為緣嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、答2　地一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標，標舉出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p786"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：應作四句。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：也可以作四句來回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨，說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或行為緣非識，謂除識所餘有支。或識非行為緣，謂無漏識及無覆無記識，除異熟生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或者行為緣而不是識，是指除了識以外，其他的名色、六入、觸、受、愛、取、有、生、老死。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或者是這了別性的識，不是福行等為緣所生，是指無漏的識及工巧處、威儀路、神通等三種無覆無記識，及除了阿賴耶識，而異熟生的前六轉識是從阿賴耶識所生不是由行為緣而生。因而說除異熟生，應更正為除異熟果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》無覆無記識除異熟生者：無覆無記識略有二種，一、異熟果，二、異熟生。當知異熟是所熏法，說行為緣。異熟生不爾，是故除之。從異熟果生，名異熟生故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無覆無記識要略而言有二種，一、異熟果，二、異熟生。應當知道異熟是由行為緣所熏生的，說它是行為緣。異熟生是前六轉識，不是行為緣所生的，應當包含在此第二句。從異熟果所生，名為異熟生。因此應當除去異熟果而非異熟生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《顯揚聖教論》卷18〈11 攝勝決擇品〉說：「謂欲界繫心有八種，一生得善心、二方便善心、三不善心、四有覆無記心、及無覆無記心，分為四種：謂異熟生心、威儀路心、工巧處心、變化心。」由此可知前六識的異熟生心也有無覆無記心，這是指聲聞、緣覺二乘之阿羅漢及辟支佛的前六轉識中一分無記心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或亦識亦行為緣，謂後有種子識及果識。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種也是識也是行為緣，是指十二支中的識支，包括後有種子識及果識：現在的阿賴耶識能攝受現在行所新熏的後有種子成隨業識，也是前生行為緣所招感的後有果識。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂後有種子識及果識者：攝受後有新生種子，是名後有種子識。現在已得生滅異熟識，是名果識。當知即是阿賴耶識，約能持種及受熏義，故得異名。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　識所攝受的後有新生種子，是名後有種子識。現在已得到的已在受用的生滅異熟識，名為果識。應當知道所說的就是阿賴耶識，這是約阿賴耶識能持種及受熏義，所以得到不同的名稱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">除如是相，是第四句。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　除了前面所說的三種相，非識亦非行為緣，非十二有支，如外稼成熟門、器世間成壞門、食任持門、威勢門、清淨門，是第四句。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、例識與名色等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例識與名色等，例說識與名色等四句的關係。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p787"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此道理，乃至觸緣受，隨其所應四句應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於這裡行緣識所說的道理，往下推理乃至觸緣受，隨其所相應的，用四句說明應該可以知道。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《成唯識論疏義演》卷10說：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、識望名色作四句：1. 有名色不以識為緣，謂佛身中無漏名色；2. 有識為緣而不是名色，謂除名色外所餘支謂六處乃至老死支，識皆與作疏遠緣故；3. 有亦識為緣亦是名色，即名色支；4. 第四句謂除前相，非十二有支。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、以名色望六處作四句：1. 有六處非以名色為緣，謂無漏六處；2. 有名色為緣而非六處，即除六處餘觸支等；3. 或亦六處亦名色為緣，謂十二支中六處支；4. 第四句除前相，非十二有支。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、六處望觸作四句：1. 有觸非六處為緣，謂無漏明相應觸；2. 觸支有六處為緣而非是觸支，即除觸支外所餘受支等；3. 有亦觸為六處為緣，即是觸支；4. 第四句除前相，非十二有支。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、觸望受為四句：1. 有受非以觸為緣，謂無漏受；2. 有以觸為緣而非是受，謂除受支外餘愛支等；3. 有亦受亦觸為緣，即是受支；4. 第四句除前相，非十二有支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由此道理至四句應知者：名色、六處、觸、受種子同時熏發，已如前釋。彼一一支為緣決擇，由行緣識道理應知。然隨所應四句差別，繁不具述。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　名色、六處、觸、受種子是同時熏發的，已如前面所解釋。其中一一支為緣的決擇，由行緣識的道理應該了知。然而隨所相應的四句差別，都是一樣的，因為很繁瑣，就不再說明了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、受與愛2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科受與愛，決擇受支與愛支，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若受為緣，皆是愛耶？設是愛者，皆受為緣耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如果以受為緣，一定都是愛嗎？如果是愛，都以受為緣嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答2　天一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標，標出四句。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：應作四句。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：應作四句來回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨，說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有是愛非受為緣，謂希求勝解脫，及依善愛而捨餘愛。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或有一種情況是愛不是以受為緣，這種愛是希求解脫生死苦惱的愛，及依出離的無漏善愛而棄捨其餘有雜染的愛。這種愛不是依三界的喜樂捨受所生的，不是追求三界殊勝果報的愛，因此說不是以受為緣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《成唯識論疏義演》卷10說：有愛非以受為緣，是指希求解脫的有漏善愛及無漏愛，此無漏善愛能壞三有，故非愛支攝，雖然也是愛，然而此愛不是煩惱等中的愛，據實而言唯以無漏中的善法欲為體，此無漏的善法欲與善愛名義相同，所以說依善愛而捨餘愛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂希求勝解脫等者：謂如無上梵行求者求無漏界，是名希求勝解脫。依善法欲，正捨家法，趣於非家，名依善愛而捨餘愛。當知此愛非受為緣，不染汙故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果是無上梵行求的人，追求無漏的涅槃界，名為希求勝解脫。依止對戒定慧聞思修的善法有強烈的願望，能捨棄煩惱的家，趣向沒有煩惱的非家而出家，名為依善愛而捨餘愛。應當知道這種愛，是出離相應，不是以受為緣，不是染汙的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p788"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或受為緣而非是愛，謂除無明觸所生受為緣，所餘有支法生。或有受為緣亦是愛，謂無明觸所生受為緣，染汙愛生。除如是相，是第四句。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或有一種情況，是受為緣而不是愛，是指除了無明觸所生的受為緣愛，以外所餘取支等，意指無明觸所生之受皆與取支乃至老死作疏遠緣。或有的情況是受為緣也是愛，是指無明觸所生受為緣，有染汙的愛生，即十二支中的愛支。除了以上的三種相，是第四句，非十二有支，如外稼成熟門、器世間成壞門、食任持門、威勢門、清淨門。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、依順後句答4　戌一、愛與取2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依順後句答，依順後句答決擇十二支，分四科；第一科愛與取，說明愛與取，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若愛為緣，皆是取耶？設是取者，皆愛為緣耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如果是愛為緣，都是取嗎？如果是取，都是愛為緣嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答3　天一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科標，標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：當知此中是順後句。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：應當知道這是隨順第二句「設是取者，皆愛為緣耶」回答，所以說是順後句。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　順後句，是指二法展轉相問，前法的範圍大，後法的範圍小，以後面的法來回答前面的問題。例如問：若愛為緣皆是取耶？設是取者皆愛為緣耶？答：所有取皆愛為緣，或愛為緣而非是取。若所提問題與順前句相反，而順應後句，且僅肯定後句之答法，例如：「凡Ｂ是Ａ，然Ａ未必是Ｂ。」名順後句。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以實例而言：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前句：是水果，一定是蘋果嗎?</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　後句：是蘋果，一定是水果嗎?</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答案：是蘋果，一定是水果；是水果，不一定是蘋果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這稱作順後句答問：水果是蘋果嗎？蘋果是水果嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂所有取皆愛為緣。或愛為緣而非是取。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是說所有的取，都是以愛為緣。或有的情況是愛為緣而不是取。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、簡</span></strong></span></span></p>
