<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科簡，簡別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂除取所餘有支，及緣善愛、勤精進等諸善法生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是指除了取以外所餘的諸有支，包括有、生及老死支，及緣出世的戒定慧等善法愛、勤精進修習三十七道品等諸善法生，雖然也是一種愛，不過是隨順無漏、出世相應，所以不是取。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》及緣善愛勤精進等諸善法生者：當知善愛，淨信所生。由此為緣，起勤精進及念、定、慧。如是諸法能對治取，是故非取，應并除之。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道善愛，是由對三寶清淨的信心所生起的。由善法愛為緣，發起勤奮精進及正念、正定、正慧。這些諸多善法能對治三有之取，因此不再有取，應該一并除去取。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、取與有2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科取與有，決擇取與有的關係，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若取為緣，皆是有耶？設是有者，皆取為緣耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如果是取為緣，都是有嗎？如果是有，一定是取為緣嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p789"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答3　天一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科標，標出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：亦應作順後句。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：也應該用順後句來回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂所有有皆取為緣。或取為緣而非是有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是指所有的有支都是以取為緣。或有的情況是取為緣而不是有支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、簡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科簡，簡別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂除有，所餘有支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是說除了有支，所餘生支及老死支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、有與生2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科有與生，決擇有支與生支，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若有為緣，皆是生耶？設是生者，皆有為緣耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如果是有為緣，都是生嗎？如果是生，都是有為緣嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答2　天一、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：諸所有生皆有為緣。或有為緣而非是生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：所有的生命體都是以有為緣。或是以有為緣而不是生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、簡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡，簡別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂除生，所餘老死最後有支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以有為緣而不是生，指除掉生，所餘老死最後有支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌四、生與老死2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科生與老死，決擇生支與老死支，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p790"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若生為緣，皆老死耶？設是老死，皆生為緣耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如果以生為緣，都是老死嗎？如果是老死，都是生為緣嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答2　天一、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：所有老死皆生為緣。或生為緣而非老死。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：所有的老死，都是以生為緣。因為沒有出生，就不會有老死。或以生為緣而非老死。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、簡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡，簡別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所謂疾病、怨憎合會、親愛別離、所求不遂，及彼所起愁歎憂苦種種熱惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是說有了生為緣就會有種種的疾病、與怨家憎恨之人和合聚會、與親近眷愛的人分別遠離、於所追求的常不順遂不能滿願，以及由這些境界所引起的悲愁、哀歎、憂傷、痛苦等種種煩惱產生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申五、所障能障分別2　酉一、所障3　戌一、障正見等2　亥一、舉於正見2　天一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科所障能障分別，約所障礙的事與能障礙的法分別，分二科；第一科所障，所障礙的事，又分三科；第一科障正見等，說明所障的正見等，又分二科；第一科舉於正見，舉出正見為例，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：是諸有支，幾與道支所攝正見為勝障礙？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：這十二有支中，哪幾支能夠對八正道的道支所攝正見，具足強而有力的障礙？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：無明，及彼所起意行、若有一分能為勝障。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：包括無明，還有因為無明而發動的意行，取所攝受的有支中一分的意業，能夠對正見具有強而有力的障礙。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》無明至能為勝障者：謂無明支，及與行支、有支一分，能為正見勝障。行支一分者，謂無明所起意行；有支一分者，謂取所攝受意業一分應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是說無明支，行支、有支一分，能夠對正見具強而有力的障礙。行支的一分，是指由無明所生起的意行；有支的一分，是說取所攝受的意業一分應該要知道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、例正思惟等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例正思惟等，例舉出正思惟等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如於正見，如是於正思惟及正精進亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如無明等障礙正見，同樣的對於正思惟及正精進也是一樣有勝障礙。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p791"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、障正語等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科障正語等，說明障正語等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若正語、正業、正命，以身行、語行及有一分為勝障礙。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於八正道中戒所攝的正語、正業、正命，以由無明發動的行支中的身行、語行、及有支中取所攝受的身語二業為勝障礙。換句話說，也就是行支中的身行、語行、及有支中取所攝受的身語二業對於正語、正業、正命有強而有力的障礙。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》以身行語行及有一分等者：身行、語行，行支一分所攝。取所攝受身語二業，有支一分所攝應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　身行、語行是行支身語意中的一部分色法所攝。取所攝受的身業、語業二種，是有支中的一部分色法所攝應當知道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、障正念等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科障正念等，說明障礙正念等支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若正念、正定，以餘有支為勝障礙應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　會障礙八正道中定所攝的正念、正定，是指除無明、行及有支以外，所餘九支為正念、正定的勝障礙應當知道。《瑜伽論記》卷3說這段文有二種解釋：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、由前所說無明、行、及有支三支說障正見、正思惟、及正精進之慧身及障正語、正業、正命之戒身故，餘九支相從總名障正定等，道理上實在唯應說愛取二支障礙八正道中的正念、正定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、定身者是心學，識支是心，名色、六處、生及老死并有心體故障定身，觸受二支是心所有，并名中色及前五處，隨識總說障正定身；愛取二支障離欲道，正障正定身，此處說正見正思惟正精進為慧學，正語正業正命為戒學，正念正定為定學。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、能障2　戌一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科能障，說明能障礙的有支，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：是諸有支，幾唯雜染品？幾通雜染、清淨品？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：於十二有支中，哪些支是屬於雜染品類？哪些是通雜染及清淨品類？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、答3　亥一、總辨品</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科總辨品，總相說明品類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：四唯雜染品，餘通雜染、清淨品。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：在十二有支中，有無明、識、愛、取，四支一定是雜染品，其餘支行、名色、六入、觸、受、愛、取、有、生、老死通於雜染品與清淨品。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷3說：為什麼說識是雜染品？答：如上文說由邪行故令心顛倒，心顛倒故，所以說識是雜染，此處據中有末心說識支，所以說無明、識、愛、取四支唯是雜染。或將識支除去說老死支是雜染，因為老死位中不能修學善法，故與雜染名。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》四唯雜染品等者：此中四言，疑應作三，謂無明、愛、取。成唯識說：三唯是染，煩惱性故；七唯不染，異熟果故。七分位中，容起染故，假說通二；餘通二種。（成唯識論八卷十一頁）由是當知此所說義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此中的四唯雜染品應該只有無明、愛、取三種，懷疑可能是譯文翻譯錯了。因為《成唯識論》卷8，11頁說：十二有支的無明、愛、取三支一定是染污的，因為它們是煩惱性。識、名色、六處、觸、受、生、老死七支一定不是染污的，因為是異熟果，是無覆無記所攝。但是這果報體七支的分位中，也能為依生起染污，所以假說通於雜染和清淨二種，所餘的行、有二支通於染淨二種。由此應當知道此處所說的義理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p792"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋妨難2　天一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋妨難，解釋難問，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：云何生支通二品耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為什麼生支通於染淨二品呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：若生惡趣及有難處，唯是雜染品；若生人天諸無難處，此通染淨品。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：如果生到三惡道去，及不能修行的處所，如地獄、畜生、餓鬼、長壽天（無想天及非非想處天）、邊地（北俱盧洲）、盲聾瘖啞、世智辯聰、佛前佛後等有難處，唯是雜染品，無法修行；如果是生在人天各個沒有聖道障難能修行處，則通於染淨二品。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、例隨應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科例隨應，例舉餘支隨所相應的品類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知餘支，隨其所應皆通二品。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　除了生支，應當知道其餘七支，隨所相應的通於染淨二品。如果遇到佛法，就有可能清淨的，如果沒有遇到佛法，就多半是染污的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若生惡趣及有難處等者：色無色界唯有難處。欲界一分亦有難處，謂生惡趣，身不清淨。若生欲界人天趣中，身清淨故，名無難處。（如顯揚十八卷十六頁說）依此差別，故說生支通染淨品。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　色界、無色界唯是有難處，主要是色界第四禪中的無想天，壽五百劫，以其心想不行，如冰魚蟄蟲，外道修行，多生其處，障於見佛、聞法，故名長壽天難。無色界的非非想處天，心不想，也不是沒有想，只有微微心，無法修行，而且八萬大劫壽，是個大障礙。生到色界或無色界的凡夫，雖然已離欲，卻容易耽著在禪定的愛味中而難以精進修行，因此算是難處。欲界一部分，如生到三惡道，果報身不清淨，地獄眾生因惡業所感，墮於彼處，長夜冥冥，受苦無間，障於見佛聞法；畜生種類不一，亦各隨因受報；或為人畜養，或居山海等處，常受鞭打殺害，又或互相吞噉，受苦無窮，障於見佛、聞法；餓鬼有三種：一其業最重者，長劫不聞漿水之名；二其業次重者，唯在人間伺求蕩滌膿血糞穢；三其業輕者，時或一飽，加以刀杖驅逼，填河塞海，受苦無量，障於見佛、聞法，因此三處都是有難處。如果生到欲界的人天趣中，果報清淨，可以見佛、聞法，名為無難處。如《顯揚聖教論》卷18，16頁所說界趣差別，因此說生支通於染淨品類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申六、不有及滅分別2　酉一、約煩惱業生雜染品辨2　戌一、舉三道理3　亥一、無明緣行2　天一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科不有及滅分別，說明還滅門，十二有支不有（種子不有）及滅（現行滅）分別，分二科；第一科約煩惱業生雜染品辨，約煩惱雜染、業雜染、生雜染，三種雜染說明還滅，又分三科；第一科舉三道理，舉出三種道理，又分三科；第一科無明緣行，說明無明緣行的不有及滅，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何等無明不有故行不有，何等無明滅故行滅耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：哪些無明沒有，則行就不會有？哪一種情況，無明滅了，行就滅了？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p793"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：有三種，發起、纏、隨眠無明。由此無明滅故，彼無明滅；由彼滅故，行亦隨滅。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：有三種無明，包括發起無明，發起福、非福、不動行的無明，即異熟果愚與勝義愚，依異熟果愚能發福行及非福行，由勝義愚能發不動行；纏無明即無明的現行；隨眠無明即無明的種子。由此隨眠無明滅故，彼纏無明、發起無明滅；由彼纏無明、發起無明滅故，行亦隨滅。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文《瑜伽論記》卷3窺基大師有二種解釋：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、有三種無明，其中發起指發業無明，這是通相應無明（異熟果愚）及不共無明（勝義愚）；纏指潤生無明，多唯相應無明，這二種都是指無明的現行；由這二種所熏成的種子名隨眠無明。由發起行的無明以一切無明為根本故，此處包括潤生無明；於潤生時行支相當有支，無明相當愛取故。又此三種無明，以發起無明為總說，發起無明中有二種，包括纏及隨眠無明，總別合論，所以說有三種。若詳細說發起之體包括與一切煩惱相應的相應無明及於四聖諦無智的不共無明，若如此說則是相應無明、不共無明、纏的潤生無明、及隨眠無明四種無明合為三種。這三種無明全部滅除故，彼發起無明滅，彼發起無明滅故，行亦隨滅。這種解釋通說發一切行之無明，因為若潤生無明未滅，由無明發起之行即不能滅。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、或另一種解釋：又有三種發起纏（煩惱現行）之隨眠無明，能發起纏的隨眠、能發起相應無明的隨眠、能發起不共無明的隨眠。此三種都是纏（現行），初纏是總說，後二相應無明及不共無明是別說。發此現行之隨眠無明有三種，由此三種隨眠無明滅故，彼現行無明滅，彼現行無明滅故行滅。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》有三種發起纏隨眠無明等者：決擇分說：或有由無明故，墮無明趣，說名愚癡；非癡所嬈，不為癡垢，非癡所媚。謂住隨眠無明。或有愚癡，為癡所嬈，不為癡垢，非癡所媚。謂由纏所攝無明。或有愚癡，為癡所嬈，為癡所垢，非癡所媚。謂由發業無明發惡業已，於此惡行而生羞恥。或有愚癡，為癡所嬈，為癡所垢，為癡所媚。謂因無明發起種種惡不善業，於此惡行無有羞恥。此中由前三種，說名愚癡，墮無明趣，不名癡人。由後一種，說名癡人。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/60.htm#7800:48738">陵本六十卷十八頁4896</a>）今於此中，且約墮無明趣說前三種，略無後一。義顯由此隨眠無明滅故，彼纏無明滅；由纏無明滅故，彼發業無明滅。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈決擇分〉說：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種情況是，或有由於無明的緣故，墮在無明類，稱為愚癡。此愚癡者的心識沒有愚癡的嬈亂；也沒有被愚癡的煩惱染汙而造業；也沒有被愚癡所迷惑而迷失；這種情況的無明，稱為住隨眠無明。這是有煩惱種子的人。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種情況是，有一類的愚癡者，被愚癡的現行所惱亂；但是沒有被愚癡所染汙而引發造業；也沒有被癡所媚惑而迷失，能夠有慚愧心，這種情況就是纏所攝的無明，就是有無明的現行而沒有造業的人。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種情況是，或有一類的愚癡者，被愚癡的現行所惱亂；被癡所垢染而引發造業；沒有被癡所媚惑而迷失，能夠生起慚愧心。這是由發業無明發惡業已，於此惡行而生羞恥慚愧的人。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四種情況是，或有一類的愚癡者，被愚癡的現行所惱亂；被愚癡所垢染而引發造業；又被癡所媚惑而迷失，對所造惡行沒有羞恥心。這是因無明發起種種惡不善業，於此惡行無有羞恥的人。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面三種人，可以說是愚癡，是屬於無明趣那一類的，由於有慚愧心，不稱為癡人。最後一種因無明發起種種惡行，不知錯，沒有羞恥心，也不會懺悔，說名為癡人。如〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷60，1986頁所說。現在此處且約墮無明趣說前三種人，省略未說後一種人。其中的義理顯示由於無明煩惱種子滅掉，無明的現行就會滅；無明的現行滅了，發業的無明就會滅，發業的無明滅，行就隨之而滅。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、行緣識2　天一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科行緣識，說明行緣識的不有及滅，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何等行不有故識不有，何等行滅故識滅耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：哪一種情況行沒有，識就沒有？哪一種情況行滅了，識即滅了嗎。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p794"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、答2　地一、舉有</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科舉有，舉出行有故識有來說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：諸行於自相續中已作已滅，及未起對治，又由意行有故，起身語行；由此有故彼有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：在相續不斷的五蘊體當中，已經造作福等諸業行雖已作已滅，已經在阿賴耶識中熏成種子（現熏種），由於沒有對治由過去造作中所熏習的種子（種生種），又當新的意行起現行（種生現），發動身語行的相續造作，又在阿賴耶識中種下新的種子（現熏種），因此行有故彼識有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》諸行於自相續中至由此有故彼有者：此顯諸行種子不斷，諸行得生；及顯意行生故，身行、語行於彼後時造作而轉；依此二義，釋由此有故彼有。諸行因已受盡，自性已滅，無間為緣，為生餘法，熏習相續，是名於自相續中已作已滅。既熏習已，未為真對治道之所對治，令永不起，是名未起對治。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡是顯示諸行的種子不曾斷除（種生種），使得諸行得生；及顯示後續的意行生起（種生現行），會推動身行、語行於後時造作生起；依這二種義理，解釋此有故彼有，此行有故彼識有。福等諸行的現行，因力已經受用殆盡，自性也已謝滅，而熏習於阿賴耶識中的種子，於沒有間斷為緣，為生餘法，不斷地種子生種子，熏習種子於阿賴耶識中，是名於自相續中已作已滅。既熏習種子以後，沒有被真正有力的對治道之所對治，使令種子永遠不再生起，是名未起對治。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、例無</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例無，例舉行無的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼無故，彼緣識亦無；此若全滅，當知識亦隨滅。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果福等諸行的種子滅了，就不會有行的現行，行的現行沒有，行緣識也就不會有了，福等諸行的種子與現行如果全部滅除，應當了知，識也就隨著滅了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、識緣名色六處觸受2　天一、舉識緣名色2　地一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科識緣名色六處觸受，說明識緣名色六處觸受的不有及滅，分二科；第一科舉識緣名色，舉出識緣名色的不有及滅，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何等識不有故名色不有，何等識滅故名色滅耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：什麼情況下識不有故名色就不有？什麼情況下染污的識滅就沒有名色呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p795"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：種子識不有故，果識不有。此俱滅故，俱名色滅。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：如果沒有種子識，就不會有果報的識，阿賴耶識的現行就沒有了。約二乘而言，阿羅漢將愛見煩惱種子斷除，縱使名言種子還在，由於沒有愛見煩惱的滋潤（緣起），不再招感下一生的果報，三界五趣的種子識沒有了，三界五趣的果報識（現行識）也沒有了，就不會有投胎的時候，也不會執著羯羅藍成為名色，所以名色也就滅了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》種子識不有故至俱名色滅者：由異熟識於現法中攝受後有新生種子，名種子識。於當生中新異熟識無間得生，是名果識。依此義說，種子識不有故，果識不有；此二滅故，名色隨滅。識與名色，名色與識，相依而轉故。於名色置有俱言，與識俱故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由今生的異熟識於現在的生命體中，能攝受後有新生種子，名為種子識。當識入母胎，下一生新的異熟識會沒有間斷的生起，稱為果識。依這裡所說的義理，種子識若沒有，果識就不會有；種子識與果識沒有，名色也隨之而滅。識要依止名色而存在，名色也要有識才能夠相續存活，這二種是相依而轉現的。因此在名色放「俱」字，是指名色與果識是同在一起的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、例緣六處等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例緣六處等，例舉出緣六處等的不有及滅。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如識望名色道理，如是餘支乃至受，隨其所應，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依識對望名色的道理。如是其他名色望六入、六入望觸、觸望受等支的關係，隨其所相應，應當知道依理可知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如識望名色道理等者：此據自體因果道理相似，故言亦爾。名色至受，皆有因果二種別故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是根據自體的因果道理相似，所以說也是如此。名色、六入、觸、受，都有因果二種差別的緣故。每一支在種子時稱為因，現行稱為果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、例餘當知3　亥一、愛緣取取緣有</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘當知，例如其餘諸支的不有及滅應當知道，分三科；第一科愛緣取取緣有，說明愛緣取、取緣有的不有及滅。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如無明緣行道理，如是愛緣取、取緣有道理，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如無明緣行的道理是這樣，如是愛種子滅故，彼愛現行滅；由彼愛現行滅故，彼取亦隨滅；取種子滅故，彼取現行滅；由彼取現行滅故，彼有亦隨滅，道理也是一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如無明緣行道理等者：此據煩惱能為雜染道理相似，故言亦爾。無明、愛、取唯雜染故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是根據煩惱能為雜染的道理相似，因為愛、取也是煩惱，由煩惱能造業，生起業（有）的雜染，所以說亦爾。無明、愛、取都是煩惱雜染，煩惱滅，就不會造業，就沒有行、有二支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p796"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、有緣生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科有緣生，說明有緣生的不有及滅。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如行緣識道理，如是有緣生，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同行緣識的道理，由生起對治故行種子滅，行種子滅故行現行滅，行現行滅故識滅，如是有滅故生滅的道理，當知也一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如行緣識道理等者：此據業果道理相似，故言亦爾。有為業因，生是彼果故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有緣生的道理也是一樣，是根據業果道理相似，所以說也是一樣。有是業因，生是業因的果。行是業，識是果。二種都是業果的關係。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、生緣老死</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科生緣老死，說明生緣老死的不有及滅。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如識緣名色道理，生緣老死，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同有識就會有名色，識滅名色就滅的道理，因此有生就會有老死，生滅老死就滅的道理也是一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如識緣名色道理等者：此據依因道理相似，故言亦爾。由生為依，老死可得故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是根據所依止因的道理是相似，所以說也是如此。因為名色是依止識，老死是依止生而有的，所以說以生為依，老死可得故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、約受雜染品辨2　戌一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約受雜染品辨，約受雜染品辨明十二支的不有及滅，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何等受不有故愛不有，何等受滅故愛滅耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：什麼樣的情況受沒有愛即沒有？什麼樣的情況受滅愛即滅嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：如行緣識道理，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：就如同以行（能引）為緣能引生識（所引）種子，由修對治道斷除行的種子，使現行的行滅了，識也就隨著滅了的道理，應當知道，依受能生愛（所生）的道理也是如此。若斷除受的種子，使受的現行滅，愛也就滅了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p797"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如行緣識道理等者：此據能引能生為緣道理相似，故言亦爾。當知此謂現法果受，非觸為緣因受。如能引行與識為緣，說名引因；如是由能生受為緣生愛，說名生因，道理亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是根據能引、能生為緣的道理相似，因此說也是如此。應當知道這是指現法果受（現行受），不是指以觸為緣的因受（種子受）。如能引的行為緣引生識種子，行是能引，識是所引，行緣識說明引因；同樣的由能生的受為緣生愛，受是能生，愛是所生，說名生因，道理也是一樣。這是根據能引能生的道理來說，如同行緣識道理,應當知道也是如此。以上是不有及滅的分別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申七、依緣起門分別2　酉一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科依緣起門分別，依緣起門作分別，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：如前所說八緣起門，幾門是十二支緣起所顯，幾門非耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如前所說的八種緣起門，哪幾門是十二支緣起所顯，哪幾門不是？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如前所說八緣起門等者：如前已說，謂依八門，緣起流轉。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/09.htm#7836:6869">陵本九卷十六頁699</a>）今此分別，幾是自身緣起所顯，幾非所顯。自身緣起，即十二支，諸有情生流轉攝故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前面卷9，288頁已說過依八種途徑，能生緣起流轉：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、內識生門，又名受用世俗境界緣起，指緣眼色生於眼識，三事和合生觸，觸為緣受生等。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、外稼成熟門，又名食因緣起，如求諸穀田種水為緣發生芽等。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、有情世間死生門，又名一切生身相續緣起，由能引能生，及一切所引所生等十二緣起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、器世間成壞門，又名一切生身依持緣起，指器世界由諸因緣施設成壞。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、食任持門，又名任持緣起，指緣四食諸根大種安住增長。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、自所作業增上勢力受用隨業所得愛非愛果門，又名一切生身差別緣起，指由不善、善有漏業，施設三惡道人天趣的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、威勢門，又名自在緣起，指善修治靜慮為緣。諸修定者隨所願樂，心想事成等。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、清淨門，又名清淨緣起，指依聽聞正法、自內如理作意，發生正見能滅無明，無明滅故諸行隨滅，廣說乃至由生滅故老死隨滅，這是還滅門。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　現在這裡分別這八門，哪些是自己生命體緣起所顯示的，哪些不是。自身緣起，是指屬於生命體緣起的十二有支，因為這是有情生死流轉所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、答2　戌一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標，標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：三門是彼所顯，謂二一分所顯，一全分所顯；餘門非。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：內識生門、自所作業增上勢力受用隨業所得愛非愛果門、有情世間死生門三門是十二緣起所顯，三門中的前二門是一部分所顯，後一門是全部所顯；其餘的門則不是。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、釋2　亥一、二一分所顯</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科二一分所顯，說明二門為十二緣起一分所顯。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為二一分所顯？謂內識生門、自業所作門。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　哪二門是十二緣起裡的一部分所顯？是指內識生門是根據六根生六識，識是識支攝緣起支不盡；自業所作增上勢力隨業所作愛非愛果門是根據從行有業生於五趣差別，不攝三煩惱及五支種子，故不全攝有支。因此說此二門是十二緣起一分所顯。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、一全分所顯</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科一全分所顯，有一門是十二緣起全分所顯的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為一全分所顯？謂有情世間轉門。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　哪一門是全分所顯？就是有情世間死生門，說明有情內身因果，也就是十二緣起。為何說其餘五門非十二支所顯呢？因為：一、外稼成熟門，二、器世間成壞門，這二類非內身因果，所以不是十二支所顯，三、食任持門，但以外食長養眾生也不是內身能生起緣，四、威勢門者，說明依禪支所得五通，通依九地發漏盡通義，因此不是十二緣起，五、清淨門，是道品無漏還滅門所攝，能滅緣起，也不是十二支所顯。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p798"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂二一分所顯等者：於八門中，內識生門、自業所作門，此二是十二支緣起一分所顯。由內識生門，唯是識支所顯；自業所作門，唯是行支所顯。又有情世間轉，此一是十二支緣起全分所顯。所餘諸門，不說自身所有緣起，故非十二支緣起所顯。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在八門中，內識生門、自業所作門，這二門是十二緣起裡面的一部分所顯示。內識生門是屬於十二有支裡面識支所顯。自業所作門，只是行支所顯。有情世間轉門，這一門是十二支緣起全部所顯。其他的門都不是說到生命體的緣起，所以不是十二有支的緣起所顯。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申八、緣起過患勝利分別2　酉一、舉過患2　戌一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科緣起過患勝利分別，說明緣起的過患勝利分別，分二科；第一科舉過患，舉出過患，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：不如實知緣起道理者，有幾種過患耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：不能如實知道緣起道理的人，有幾種過失災患呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、答2　亥一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標，標出五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：有五。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：會有五種過失災患。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、列2　天一、初四過患2　地一、舉由我見及前際俱行見</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出來，分二科；第一科初四過患，說明前四種過患，又分二科；第一科舉有我見及前際俱行見，舉出有我見及前際俱行見的過患。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂起我見，及能發起前際俱行見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能生起我見，及能發起前際俱行見二種過患。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷3窺基大師說：不能如實知道緣起道理的人，會於五陰中妄計有身，強立主宰，恒起我見，執我、我所，或計執一陰為我，餘四陰為我所等；又能於過去生的五陰依止我見生起斷見、常見及邪見。　　</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、例後際俱行見等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例後際俱行見等，例說後際俱行見等過患。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如前際俱行見，如是後際俱行見、前後際俱行見亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　只要有我見，對過去生的五蘊生起斷見、常見及邪見，對來生的五蘊及現在生的五蘊也會生起斷見、常見及邪見。六十二見中，隨其所相應，緣於三際，生起常見、斷見及邪見，這三見加上我見就有四種過患。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、第五過患</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第五過患，說明最後一個過患。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p799"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於彼見猛利堅執，有取有怖，於現法中不般涅槃，是名第五過患。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又對於我見、常見、斷見、及邪見的思想，猛利堅固執著，於此四見取著為最殊勝生起見取，怖畏涅槃，於現法中不得涅槃，或生起邪見中的五種現法涅槃論，這就是第五種過患。總之不能如實知道緣起道理的人，能生我見、常見、斷見、見取見及邪見，而有五種過患。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》不如實知緣起道理等者：此有五種過患。一、起我見；二、能發起前際俱行見；三、能發起後際俱行見；四、能發起前後際俱行見；五、於彼見猛利堅執，有取有怖，於現法中不般涅槃。此中彼見，謂即我見、前際見等。由於前際俱行見等猛利堅執，故說有取。由於我見猛利堅執，故說有怖。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不如實知緣起道理的人，有五種過患。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、生起我見。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、能發起前際俱行見，對過去生有我見同時生起，由此引生常見、斷見、或是邪見；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、能發起後際俱行見，對來生也會依於我見引生常見、斷見或是邪見；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、能發起前後際俱行見，於今生也會依於我見引生常見、斷見或是邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、於彼我見、常見、斷見、或是邪見猛利堅固執著，有取著有怖畏，於現法中不般涅槃。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此文中所說彼見，是指我見、前際見等。這裡的彼見，是對前面的四種見猛利堅持。由於對三時的我見等猛利堅持所以說是有取，由於對我見等有強烈的執取，所以說有怖。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、例勝利2　戌一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例勝利，例舉勝利，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：如實知者，有幾種勝利耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如實知道緣起的道理的人，可以有幾種殊勝的利益呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：翻前五過，應知勝利亦有五種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：與前面五種過失反過來，應該知道殊勝的利益也有五種，如實了知緣起，由此可以知道過去、現在、未來只是惑、業、苦的流轉，不會生起我見、常見、斷見、邪見及見取見等五種過患。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申九、諸門分別14　酉一、實非實有攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科諸門分別，再以十四種角度來分別十二緣起，分十四科；第一科實非實有攝，說明實及非實有所攝支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，是十二支緣起，幾支是實有？謂九。幾支非實有？謂餘。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，這十二支緣起，哪幾支是實有？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是實有及假有，據〈決擇‧思所成慧地〉卷65說：若諸法不待所餘、不依所餘施設自相，應知略說是實有相。若法本身有自己的體相，是實有法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若有諸法待於所餘、依於所餘施設自相，應知略說是假有相，非實物有。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　非實：是複合物，要有很多支組合才能形成，是假安立，是一種概念。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　包括無明、行次第乃至取等九支。哪幾支非實有？其餘指有、生、老死三支不是實有。有支是由行、識、名色、六入、觸、受六支和合而成的種子狀態，生支及老死支是有的現行，因此有、生、老死這三支不是實有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p800"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》是十二支緣起幾支是實有等者：有、生、老死三是非實有。成唯識云：已潤六支合為有故；即識等五三相位別，名生等故。準彼應釋。（成唯識論八卷十一頁）餘九實有，易可了知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有、生、老死這三支不是實有。《成唯識論》說：已被愛取滋潤的行、識、名色、六入、觸、受六支合稱為有；即識名色六入觸受這五法，有三種相狀階位差別，名為生等故。應參照《成唯識論》卷8，11頁的解釋。剩餘九支是實有，容易了知不再多說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、一事非一事攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科一事非一事攝，說明一事非一事所攝支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">幾一事為自性？謂五。幾非一事為自性？謂餘。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　幾支是以一事為自性？事即是體，以一法為體獨自一支，名一事為自性。一事，即無明、識、觸、受、愛五支。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　幾支不是一事為自性，二法以上為體，即名非一事。因此其餘七支不是一事為自性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾一事為自性等者：此中五是一事，謂無明、識、觸、受、愛五，餘非一事。亦如成唯識說。（成唯識論八卷十一頁）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這其中五支是一事，指無明、識、觸、受、愛五支，都只有一事。其餘支不只一事。也如《成唯識論》卷8，11頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　例如行支包括身、語、意三種；名色包括受想行識的名及色，共有五法；六入包括眼耳鼻舌身意六處；取包括欲取、見取、戒禁取、我語取四取；有包括：行識名色六入觸受六法；生及老死也是識名色六入觸受五法種子的現行等有三種相狀位階差別，所以這七支不是一事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、所知障因攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科所知障因攝，說明所知障因所攝支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="36664:7869"></a>幾是所知障因？謂一。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　幾支是所知障因？唯無明一支。這裡說的所知障因一支，是指無明支。由於無明對於所知能障覆真實，因此名為所知障的因。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以大乘來說要斷煩惱障及所知障。煩惱障去除，可以成就阿羅漢果。成就阿羅漢果還有法執的所知障，執著法是真實的，菩薩還要斷除所知障才能圓滿的度化眾生，成就佛道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾是所知障因謂一者：此謂無明。由於所知障覆真實，是故名為所知障因。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡說的所知障因一支，是指無明支。由於無明對於所知能障覆真實，因此名為所知障的因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉四、苦因果攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科苦因果攝，說明苦因與苦果所攝支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">幾能生苦？謂五。幾苦胎藏？謂五。幾唯是苦？謂二。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十二支中幾支能生苦？十二支裡面有五支，是能使令有情產生苦果的，指無明、行、愛、取、有五支。無明愛取是惑，行與有是業，有惑及業產生苦。無明行是引因，能引發苦果的因。愛取有是能生，能夠將之前所引發的滋潤起現行，所以這五支能生苦。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　幾支是苦胎藏？胎藏其實是指因（種子），苦的因。就是苦還在胎裡面隱藏，還是種子的狀態，包括識、名色、六入、觸、受的種子五支。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　幾支唯是苦？苦胎藏現行（苦種子現行），是指生老死，老死是伴隨生。有生即有種種的苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p801"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾能生苦等者：五能生苦，謂無明、行、愛、取、有五。苦胎藏，謂識乃至受五法種子。二唯是苦，謂生、老死。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十二支裡面有五支，是能使令有情產生苦果的，指無明、行、愛、取、有五支，就是惑及業，無明愛取是惑，行和有是業，這五支可以使令有情產生苦。苦胎藏，就是苦還在胎裡面隱藏，是指識乃至受五法種子，還在種子的狀態稱為苦胎藏。二支唯是苦，是說生、老死一定是苦的，因為種子現行了，生就是苦，有生就有種種的苦。老死也是苦，大家都不願意，沒有人願意老死。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉五、因果分等攝3　戌一、因分</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科因果分等攝，說明因分與果分等所攝支，分三科；第一科因分，說明因分所攝支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">幾說為因分？謂前六，無明乃至觸，及愛、取、有三，說為因分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十二支中哪幾支說為因分？是指前六支的無明乃至觸，及愛、取、有三支，共有九支說為因分。無明與行能引發五法種子，識、名色、六入、觸是所引，五法種子未現行也都稱為因。愛、取、有這三支能生果，也可以稱為因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、果分</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科果分，說明果分所攝支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">幾說為果分？謂後二說為果分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十二支中哪幾支是屬於果報的？十二緣起強調苦果，生與老死後二支，稱為果分。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、雜因果分2　亥一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科雜因果分，說明雜因果分所攝支，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">幾說為雜因果分？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十二支中哪幾支是屬於雜因果分，屬於因也屬於果的支分？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋3　天一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科標，標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂所餘支說為雜分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所餘支即受支說為雜分。受支，也是因也是果，叫雜因果分。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p802"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">有二種受名為雜分。一、謂後法以觸為緣因受；二、謂現法與愛為緣果受；此二雜說為觸緣受。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有二種受名為雜分。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、是對後法以觸為緣的因受，（觸的後法是指受，以觸為緣才有受，但都還在種子的狀態名因受）主要是說觸種子所攝受的受種子。無明緣行會發動造業，發動造業會熏習識名色六處觸受五法種子，雖然五法是同時熏成，本無前後，但就未來生起果報的時候它有前後的次序，所以種子也方便說有前後，先有識出現才有名色出現，名色是攝受在識當中，乃至以觸為緣才有受，因此受的種子也含攝在觸種子之後，所以說觸種子所攝受的種子受。所謂種子受即是因受。是說受種子現階段是因，將來它會生起受的現行，受的現行是屬於後法，未來的果報；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、現法中與愛為緣的果受，現在現行的受，會使令有情對境界產生和合愛或別離愛等，好的境界希望和合，壞的境界希望別離，得到的感受即是果報，所以說這是果受。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷3解釋：「有二種受名為雜分。一謂後法以觸為緣因受者，謂受種子以觸種子為因，望後際果是其因受。二謂現法與愛為緣果受者，現起報受作緣生愛，是前際家果故名果受。故此一受雜因果分。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂所餘支說為雜分等者：除前所說，唯餘受支名所餘支。受有二種，若觸種子所攝受種子受，是謂後法以觸為緣因受；若於現法無明觸所生受，能生貪愛，是謂現法與愛為緣果受。由是差別，受名雜分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　除了前面所說的，唯有受支稱為所餘支。受有二種，若是觸種子所攝受的種子受，是指下一世以觸為緣的因受；如果是於現法中無明觸所生的受，能引生貪愛，是指現法與愛為緣的果報受。所以受是通於因果的，有受就會有煩惱，有煩惱會推動去造業，造業的同時就熏習了種子，就是下一生的因受。由這種差別，受名為雜分。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉六、能生二果攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科能生二果攝，說明能生二果所攝支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，幾支能生愛非愛境界果？幾支能生自體果？謂前六支能生前果，後三支能生後果，一支俱生二果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，十二緣起裡面，哪幾支能生出屬於別報的可愛及不可愛的境界果？哪幾支能生出屬於正報的自體果？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一個問題，幾支能生愛非愛境界果？愛非愛是在十二支中哪一支才會得到？是在受。當六根接觸六境引發六識，引發六識時又在六境中起分別，所以六處緣觸，依無明觸所生的受，有樂受苦受不苦不樂受，這裡強調樂受苦受，當樂受苦受出現的時候，它本身即是一種果報，相對於異熟果來說，名境界果。為什麼？因為樂受苦受是攀緣外在的境界才會出現，它不是自體的感受。受能生愛非愛的境界果。前六支能生起受，所以前六支能境界果。無明行是能引發愛非愛境界果的因，識名色六處是愛非愛境界果發生的依止處，觸是生起受主要的因，所以前六支能生前果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二個問題，幾支能生自體果（異熟果）？自體果，生及老死。自體果是由誰而生，是由愛取有；愛、取能滋潤五法種子使令有情得到下一個生命體的果報。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　「一支俱生二果。」受支能生起二種果。因為如前說受可分為因受果受，因受即是受種子，受種子能生起受，當受出生本身即是愛非愛境界果；當受現行時，為緣生起愛，愛緣取取緣有，會生起生及死的自體果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂前六支能生前果等者：無明至觸，名前六支，由此能生愛非愛境界果；愛、取、有三，名後三支，由此能生自體果；中間受支，俱生二果。由是說有境界、自體二受差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無明、行、識、名色、六入、觸，名為前六支，由這六支能生愛非愛的境界果；愛、取、有三支，名為後三支，由這三支能生自體果；中間的受支，能生二種果，因此說有境界受與自體受二種受的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉七、受俱不俱攝4　戌一、樂受俱行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科受俱不俱攝，說明受俱不俱所攝支，分四科；第一科樂受俱行，說明樂受俱行所攝支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，幾支樂受俱行？謂除二，所餘支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，十二有支中幾支是樂受俱行？是指除了受支與老死支二支以外，因為不同的二支在一起才稱為俱行，受支不說與受本身俱行，老死位中多分無樂及捨受故，其餘十支都可能是樂受俱行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、苦受俱行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科苦受俱行，說明有苦受俱行支所攝支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="10p803"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">幾支苦受俱行？謂即彼及所除中一。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十二支中幾支是苦受俱行？彼是指跟樂受俱行的那十支，樂受中所排除的其中一支，也就是老死支。所以彼樂受俱行的十支，加上老死支，總共有十一支。這十一支是跟苦受俱行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、不苦不樂受俱行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科不苦不樂受俱行，說明不苦不樂受俱行所攝支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">幾支不苦不樂受俱行？謂如樂受道理應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十二支中幾支是不苦不樂受俱行？如同樂受的道理應該知道。就是除掉受支與老死支以外，其餘十支，都有可能與不苦不樂受相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌四、不與受俱行</span></strong></span></span></p>
